00113 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function perfEma(prev, sample)
00114 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not sample or sample <= 0 then
00115 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return prev or 0
00116 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
00117 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not prev or prev <= 0 then
00118 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return sample
00119 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
00120 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local alpha = PERF_MONITOR_ALPHA or 0.25
00121 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return prev + (sample - prev) * alpha
00122 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end

00152 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function perfMonitorSetRayInfo(baseIdx, effIdx, useFixed)
00153 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local baseLabel = "-"
00154 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local effLabel = "-"
00155 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if RAY_PRESETS and #RAY_PRESETS > 0 then
00156 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local n = #RAY_PRESETS
00157 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local b = baseIdx or RAY_PRESET_INDEX or 1
00158 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local e = effIdx or b
00159 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if b < 1 then b = 1 elseif b > n then b = n end
00160 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if e < 1 then e = 1 elseif e > n then e = n end
00161 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         baseLabel = (RAY_PRESETS[b] and RAY_PRESETS[b].label) or tostring(b)
00162 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         effLabel = (RAY_PRESETS[e] and RAY_PRESETS[e].label) or tostring(e)
00163 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
00164 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     PERF_MONITOR_LAST_BASE_RAY_LABEL = baseLabel
00165 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     PERF_MONITOR_LAST_EFFECTIVE_RAY_LABEL = effLabel
00166 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     PERF_MONITOR_LAST_RAYCAST_MODE = useFixed and "FIXED" or "FLOAT"
00167 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end

00173 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     PERF_MONITOR_EMA_FRAME_US = perfEma(PERF_MONITOR_EMA_FRAME_US, frame)
00174 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
00175 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if PERF_MONITOR_ACTIVE_SAMPLE then

00187 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
00188 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local nowUs = frameNowUs or perfNowUs()
00189 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not DEBUG_PERF_MONITOR or not enablePerfLogs or not nowUs then
00190 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return

00192 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if PERF_MONITOR_LAST_LOG_US == 0 then

00196 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local dbufStatus = getDoubleBufferStatusLabel()
00197 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         logPerf(string.format(

00199 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             (PERF_MONITOR_EMA_FRAME_US or 0) / 1000.0,
00200 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             (PERF_MONITOR_EMA_RAYCAST_US or 0) / 1000.0,
00201 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             (PERF_MONITOR_EMA_WALL_US or 0) / 1000.0,
00202 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             (PERF_MONITOR_EMA_FOG_US or 0) / 1000.0,

00205 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             (PERF_MONITOR_EMA_SIM_US or 0) / 1000.0,

00210 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             tostring(PERF_MONITOR_LAST_BASE_RAY_LABEL or "-"),
00211 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             tostring(PERF_MONITOR_LAST_EFFECTIVE_RAY_LABEL or "-"),

00228 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function readMemoryStats()
00229 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local stats = {}
00230 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not vmupro or not vmupro.system then
00231 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return stats
00232 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
00233 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if vmupro.system.getMemoryUsage then
00234 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local ok, value = pcall(vmupro.system.getMemoryUsage)
00235 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if ok and value then
00236 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             stats.usage = value
00237 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
00238 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end

00267 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function applyDoubleBufferMode(enable)
00268 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local wantEnable = enable == true
00269 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if wantEnable then
00270 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if DOUBLE_BUFFER_ACTIVE then return true end
00271 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if not vmupro or not vmupro.graphics or not vmupro.graphics.startDoubleBufferRenderer then
00272 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             DOUBLE_BUFFER_ACTIVE = false
00273 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             return false
00274 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
00275 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local offStats = readMemoryStats()
00276 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if offStats.usage then DOUBLE_BUFFER_OFF_USAGE_BYTES = offStats.usage end
00277 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if offStats.largest then DOUBLE_BUFFER_OFF_LARGEST_BYTES = offStats.largest end
00278 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local okStart, errStart = pcall(vmupro.graphics.startDoubleBufferRenderer)
00279 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if not okStart then
00280 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             DOUBLE_BUFFER_ACTIVE = false
00281 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local warnLevel = (vmupro and vmupro.system and vmupro.system.LOG_WARN) or 1
00282 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             logBoot(warnLevel, "startDoubleBufferRenderer failed: " .. tostring(errStart))
00283 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             return false
00284 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
00285 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         DOUBLE_BUFFER_ACTIVE = true
00286 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local onStats = readMemoryStats()
00287 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if onStats.usage then DOUBLE_BUFFER_ON_USAGE_BYTES = onStats.usage end
00288 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if onStats.largest then DOUBLE_BUFFER_ON_LARGEST_BYTES = onStats.largest end
00289 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         updateDoubleBufferDeltas()
00290 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if enablePerfLogs then

00292 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 "DBUF ON deltaUsage=%dB deltaLargest=%dB",
00293 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 DOUBLE_BUFFER_DELTA_USAGE_BYTES or 0,
00294 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 DOUBLE_BUFFER_DELTA_LARGEST_BYTES or 0
00295 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             ))
00296 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
00297 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return true
00298 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
00299 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
00300 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if DOUBLE_BUFFER_ACTIVE and vmupro and vmupro.graphics and vmupro.graphics.stopDoubleBufferRenderer then
00301 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local okStop, errStop = pcall(vmupro.graphics.stopDoubleBufferRenderer)
00302 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if not okStop then

00305 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
00306 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
00307 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     DOUBLE_BUFFER_ACTIVE = false
00308 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local offStats = readMemoryStats()
00309 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if offStats.usage then DOUBLE_BUFFER_OFF_USAGE_BYTES = offStats.usage end
00310 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if offStats.largest then DOUBLE_BUFFER_OFF_LARGEST_BYTES = offStats.largest end
00311 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     updateDoubleBufferDeltas()

00313 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         logPerf(string.format(
00314 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             "DBUF OFF deltaUsage=%dB deltaLargest=%dB",

00317 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         ))
00318 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
00319 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return true
00320 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end

00385 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] -- Safety Check Functions
00386 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function safeLog(level, message)
00387 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not enableBootLogs then return end
00388 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if vmupro.system.log then
00389 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local lvl = vmupro.system.LOG_INFO
00390 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if level == "ERROR" then
00391 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             lvl = vmupro.system.LOG_ERROR
00392 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         elseif level == "WARN" then
00393 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             lvl = vmupro.system.LOG_WARN
00394 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         elseif level == "DEBUG" then
00395 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             lvl = vmupro.system.LOG_DEBUG
00396 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
00397 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         vmupro.system.log(lvl, "SAFETY", message)
00398 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     else
00399 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         print("[SAFETY " .. level .. "] " .. message)
00400 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
00401 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end

00403 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function validateSprite(sprite, context)
00404 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not sprite then
00405 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         safeLog("ERROR", "Sprite is nil in context: " .. (context or "unknown"))
00406 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return false
00407 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
00408 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not sprite.width or not sprite.height then
00409 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         safeLog("ERROR", "Sprite missing width/height in context: " .. (context or "unknown"))
00410 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return false
00411 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
00412 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if sprite.width <= 0 or sprite.height <= 0 then
00413 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         safeLog("ERROR", "Sprite has invalid dimensions in context: " .. (context or "unknown") ..
00414 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                " width=" .. tostring(sprite.width) .. " height=" .. tostring(sprite.height))
00415 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return false
00416 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
00417 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return true
00418 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end

00420 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function validateTextureDimensions(sprite, context)
00421 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not validateSprite(sprite, context) then
00422 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return false
00423 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
00424 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if sprite.width > 2048 or sprite.height > 2048 then
00425 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         safeLog("WARN", "Texture dimensions may be too large in context: " .. (context or "unknown") ..
00426 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                " width=" .. tostring(sprite.width) .. " height=" .. tostring(sprite.height))
00427 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
00428 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return true

00431 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function safeDivide(value, divisor, context)
00432 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if divisor == 0 then
00433 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         safeLog("ERROR", "Division by zero in context: " .. (context or "unknown") ..
00434 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                " value=" .. tostring(value) .. " divisor=0")
00435 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return 0
00436 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
00437 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return value / divisor
00438 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end

00440 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function checkArrayBounds(array, index, context)
00441 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not array then
00442 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         safeLog("ERROR", "Array is nil in context: " .. (context or "unknown"))
00443 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return false
00444 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
00445 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local length = #array
00446 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if index < 1 or index > length then
00447 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         safeLog("ERROR", "Array index out of bounds in context: " .. (context or "unknown") ..
00448 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                " index=" .. tostring(index) .. " length=" .. tostring(length))
00449 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return false
00450 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
00451 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return true
00452 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end

00454 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function safeScale(sprite, scaleX, scaleY, context)
00455 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not validateSprite(sprite, context) then
00456 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return false
00457 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
00458 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if type(scaleX) ~= "number" or type(scaleY) ~= "number" then
00459 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         safeLog("ERROR", "Scale values are not numbers in context: " .. (context or "unknown") ..
00460 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                " scaleX=" .. tostring(scaleX) .. " scaleY=" .. tostring(scaleY))
00461 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return false
00462 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
00463 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if scaleX < 0 or scaleY < 0 then
00464 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         safeLog("WARN", "Negative scale values in context: " .. (context or "unknown") ..
00465 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                " scaleX=" .. tostring(scaleX) .. " scaleY=" .. tostring(scaleY))
00466 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
00467 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return true
00468 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end

00536 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
00537 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function buildSingleRoomMap()
00538 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local mapOut = {}
00539 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     for y = 0, 15 do
00540 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local row = {}
00541 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         for x = 0, 15 do
00542 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if x == 0 or x == 15 or y == 0 or y == 15 then
00543 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 row[#row + 1] = 1
00544 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             else
00545 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 row[#row + 1] = 0
00546 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             end
00547 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
00548 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         mapOut[#mapOut + 1] = row
00549 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
00550 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return mapOut
00551 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end

00686 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] function getLevelLabel(levelId)
00687 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     for i = 1, #LEVEL_SELECT_LIST do
00688 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local entry = LEVEL_SELECT_LIST[i]
00689 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if entry and entry.id == levelId then
00690 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             return entry.label
00691 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
00692 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
00693 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return tostring(levelId)
00694 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end

00925 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function bootstrapExpansionDataLayer()
00926 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not ExpansionRuntimeState or not ExpansionRuntimeState.bootstrap then
00927 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return
00928 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
00929 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local state = ExpansionRuntimeState.bootstrap()
00930 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not state then
00931 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return
00932 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
00933 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     player_build_state = state.player_build_state or player_build_state
00934 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     inventory_state = state.inventory_state or inventory_state
00935 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     stash_state = state.stash_state or stash_state
00936 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     achievement_state = state.achievement_state or achievement_state
00937 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     high_score_state = state.high_score_state or high_score_state
00938 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     score_state = state.score_state or score_state
00939 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end
00940 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
00941 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function beginExpansionRun(levelId)
00942 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not ExpansionRuntimeState or not ExpansionRuntimeState.beginRun then
00943 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return
00944 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
00945 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local state = ExpansionRuntimeState.beginRun(levelId, currentLevel)
00946 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not state then
00947 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return
00948 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
00949 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     player_build_state = state.player_build_state or player_build_state
00950 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     inventory_state = state.inventory_state or inventory_state
00951 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     stash_state = state.stash_state or stash_state
00952 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     achievement_state = state.achievement_state or achievement_state
00953 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     high_score_state = state.high_score_state or high_score_state
00954 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     score_state = state.score_state or score_state
00955 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end
00956 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function wallQuadLog(msg)
00957 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if enableBootLogs and DEBUG_WALL_QUADS_LOG and wallQuadLogCount < 30 then
00958 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         print(msg)
00959 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         wallQuadLogCount = wallQuadLogCount + 1
00960 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
00961 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end
00962 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
00963 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function forceSpriteColorKey(sprite, label)
00964 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not sprite then
00965 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return
00966 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
00967 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if sprite.transparentColor == nil then
00968 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return
00969 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
00970 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local before = sprite.transparentColor

00974 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         "[SAFETY] [TEX] %s colorKey=0x%04X -> 0x%04X",
00975 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         tostring(label or "sprite"), before, after
00976 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     ))
00977 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end

01010 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function setAudioMixHz(hz)
01011 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local target = hz or 60
01012 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local idx = 1
01013 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local bestDelta = math.abs((AUDIO_MIX_HZ_PRESETS[1] or target) - target)
01014 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     for i = 2, #AUDIO_MIX_HZ_PRESETS do
01015 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local delta = math.abs((AUDIO_MIX_HZ_PRESETS[i] or target) - target)
01016 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if delta < bestDelta then
01017 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             bestDelta = delta
01018 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             idx = i
01019 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
01020 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01021 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     AUDIO_MIX_HZ_INDEX = idx
01022 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     AUDIO_UPDATE_TARGET_HZ = AUDIO_MIX_HZ_PRESETS[idx]
01023 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     AUDIO_UPDATE_STEP_US = math.floor(1000000 / AUDIO_UPDATE_TARGET_HZ)
01024 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end

01040 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function stepDebugPage(delta)
01041 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local pages = {DEBUG_PAGE_CORE, DEBUG_PAGE_VIDEO, DEBUG_PAGE_PERF}
01042 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local current = 1
01043 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     for i = 1, #pages do
01044 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if pages[i] == titleDebugPage then
01045 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             current = i
01046 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             break
01047 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
01048 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01049 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local nextIdx = current + (delta or 1)
01050 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if nextIdx < 1 then nextIdx = #pages end
01051 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if nextIdx > #pages then nextIdx = 1 end
01052 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     titleDebugPage = pages[nextIdx]
01053 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     titleDebugSelection = 1
01054 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end

01066 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function nearestPresetIndex(list, target)
01067 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not list or #list == 0 then return 1 end
01068 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local bestIdx = 1
01069 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local bestDelta = math.abs((list[1] or target) - target)
01070 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     for i = 2, #list do
01071 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local delta = math.abs((list[i] or target) - target)
01072 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if delta < bestDelta then
01073 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             bestDelta = delta
01074 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             bestIdx = i
01075 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
01076 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01077 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return bestIdx
01078 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end

01080 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function nearestRayPresetIndex(targetRays)
01081 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not RAY_PRESETS or #RAY_PRESETS == 0 then
01082 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return 1
01083 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01084 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local bestIdx = 1
01085 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local bestDelta = math.abs((RAY_PRESETS[1].rays or targetRays) - targetRays)
01086 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     for i = 2, #RAY_PRESETS do
01087 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local delta = math.abs((RAY_PRESETS[i].rays or targetRays) - targetRays)
01088 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if delta < bestDelta then
01089 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             bestDelta = delta
01090 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             bestIdx = i
01091 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
01092 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01093 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return bestIdx
01094 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end

01096 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function clampInt(v, minV, maxV)
01097 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if v < minV then return minV end
01098 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if v > maxV then return maxV end
01099 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return v
01100 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end

01102 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function refreshExpViewDistance()
01103 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local texDist = EXP_TEX_MAX_DIST or DRAW_DIST_PRESETS[DRAW_DIST_INDEX] or 8.0
01104 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local viewDist = texDist
01105 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not DEBUG_DISABLE_FOG then
01106 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local fogEnd = FOG_END or texDist
01107 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local fogView = fogEnd + 0.5
01108 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if fogView > viewDist then
01109 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             viewDist = fogView
01110 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
01111 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01112 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local maxFogPreset = (FOG_DISTANCE_PRESETS and FOG_DISTANCE_PRESETS[#FOG_DISTANCE_PRESETS]) or 28.0
01113 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if viewDist > maxFogPreset then
01114 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         viewDist = maxFogPreset
01115 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01116 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     EXP_VIEW_DIST = viewDist
01117 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end
01118 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
01119 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function normalizeFogRange()
01120 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not FOG_START_PRESETS or not FOG_END_PRESETS then return end
01121 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not FOG_START_INDEX then FOG_START_INDEX = 1 end
01122 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not FOG_END_INDEX then FOG_END_INDEX = 1 end
01123 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if FOG_START_INDEX < 1 then FOG_START_INDEX = 1 end
01124 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if FOG_END_INDEX < 1 then FOG_END_INDEX = 1 end
01125 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if FOG_START_INDEX > #FOG_START_PRESETS then FOG_START_INDEX = #FOG_START_PRESETS end
01126 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if FOG_END_INDEX > #FOG_END_PRESETS then FOG_END_INDEX = #FOG_END_PRESETS end
01127 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
01128 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if FOG_END_INDEX <= FOG_START_INDEX then
01129 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         FOG_END_INDEX = FOG_START_INDEX + 1
01130 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if FOG_END_INDEX > #FOG_END_PRESETS then
01131 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             FOG_END_INDEX = #FOG_END_PRESETS
01132 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             FOG_START_INDEX = math.max(1, FOG_END_INDEX - 1)
01133 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
01134 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01135 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
01136 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     FOG_START = FOG_START_PRESETS[FOG_START_INDEX]
01137 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     FOG_END = FOG_END_PRESETS[FOG_END_INDEX]
01138 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if FOG_END <= FOG_START then
01139 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         FOG_END = FOG_START + 0.5
01140 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01141 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     refreshExpViewDistance()
01142 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end
01143 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
01144 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function normalizeMipmapRanges()
01145 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not MIPMAP_DIST_PRESETS or #MIPMAP_DIST_PRESETS == 0 then return end
01146 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local n = #MIPMAP_DIST_PRESETS
01147 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not MIPMAP1_DIST_INDEX then MIPMAP1_DIST_INDEX = 1 end
01148 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not MIPMAP2_DIST_INDEX then MIPMAP2_DIST_INDEX = math.min(n, 2) end
01149 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not MIPMAP3_DIST_INDEX then MIPMAP3_DIST_INDEX = math.min(n, 3) end
01150 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not MIPMAP4_DIST_INDEX then MIPMAP4_DIST_INDEX = math.min(n, 4) end
01151 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
01152 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if n == 1 then
01153 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         MIPMAP1_DIST_INDEX = 1
01154 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         MIPMAP2_DIST_INDEX = 1
01155 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         MIPMAP3_DIST_INDEX = 1
01156 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         MIPMAP4_DIST_INDEX = 1
01157 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     elseif n == 2 then
01158 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         MIPMAP1_DIST_INDEX = clampInt(MIPMAP1_DIST_INDEX, 1, 1)
01159 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         MIPMAP2_DIST_INDEX = clampInt(MIPMAP2_DIST_INDEX, 2, 2)
01160 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         MIPMAP3_DIST_INDEX = clampInt(MIPMAP3_DIST_INDEX, 2, 2)
01161 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         MIPMAP4_DIST_INDEX = clampInt(MIPMAP4_DIST_INDEX, 2, 2)
01162 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     elseif n == 3 then
01163 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         MIPMAP1_DIST_INDEX = clampInt(MIPMAP1_DIST_INDEX, 1, 1)
01164 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         MIPMAP2_DIST_INDEX = clampInt(MIPMAP2_DIST_INDEX, 2, 2)
01165 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         MIPMAP3_DIST_INDEX = clampInt(MIPMAP3_DIST_INDEX, 3, 3)
01166 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         MIPMAP4_DIST_INDEX = clampInt(MIPMAP4_DIST_INDEX, 3, 3)
01167 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     else
01168 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         -- Keep strict ordering without pushing unrelated levels to max.
01169 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         MIPMAP1_DIST_INDEX = clampInt(MIPMAP1_DIST_INDEX, 1, n - 3)
01170 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         MIPMAP2_DIST_INDEX = clampInt(MIPMAP2_DIST_INDEX, MIPMAP1_DIST_INDEX + 1, n - 2)
01171 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         MIPMAP3_DIST_INDEX = clampInt(MIPMAP3_DIST_INDEX, MIPMAP2_DIST_INDEX + 1, n - 1)
01172 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         MIPMAP4_DIST_INDEX = clampInt(MIPMAP4_DIST_INDEX, MIPMAP3_DIST_INDEX + 1, n)
01173 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01174 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
01175 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     WALL_MIPMAP_DIST1 = MIPMAP_DIST_PRESETS[MIPMAP1_DIST_INDEX]
01176 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     WALL_MIPMAP_DIST2 = MIPMAP_DIST_PRESETS[MIPMAP2_DIST_INDEX]
01177 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     WALL_MIPMAP_DIST3 = MIPMAP_DIST_PRESETS[MIPMAP3_DIST_INDEX]
01178 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     WALL_MIPMAP_DIST4 = MIPMAP_DIST_PRESETS[MIPMAP4_DIST_INDEX]
01179 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end

01195 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function applyPerfQualityPreset(newIndex)
01196 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not PERF_QUALITY_PRESETS or #PERF_QUALITY_PRESETS == 0 then
01197 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return
01198 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01199 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     PERF_QUALITY_INDEX = clampInt(newIndex or PERF_QUALITY_INDEX or 1, 1, #PERF_QUALITY_PRESETS)
01200 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local preset = PERF_QUALITY_PRESETS[PERF_QUALITY_INDEX]
01201 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
01202 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if preset == "QUALITY" then
01203 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         LOW_RES_MODE = "quality"
01204 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         RAY_PRESET_INDEX = nearestRayPresetIndex(120)
01205 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         DRAW_DIST_INDEX = nearestPresetIndex(DRAW_DIST_PRESETS, 16)
01206 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         FAR_TEX_OFF_INDEX = nearestPresetIndex(FAR_TEX_OFF_PRESETS, 999)
01207 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         WALL_MIPMAP_ENABLED = true
01208 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         MIP_LOD_ENABLED = true
01209 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         FOG_DITHER_SIZE_INDEX = nearestPresetIndex(FOG_DITHER_SIZE_PRESETS, 2)
01210 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     elseif preset == "PERFORMANCE" then
01211 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         LOW_RES_MODE = "fast"
01212 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         RAY_PRESET_INDEX = nearestRayPresetIndex(48)
01213 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         DRAW_DIST_INDEX = nearestPresetIndex(DRAW_DIST_PRESETS, 8)
01214 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         FAR_TEX_OFF_INDEX = nearestPresetIndex(FAR_TEX_OFF_PRESETS, 10)
01215 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         WALL_MIPMAP_ENABLED = true
01216 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         MIP_LOD_ENABLED = true
01217 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         FOG_DITHER_SIZE_INDEX = nearestPresetIndex(FOG_DITHER_SIZE_PRESETS, 4)
01218 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     else
01219 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         -- BALANCED default
01220 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         LOW_RES_MODE = "quality"
01221 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         RAY_PRESET_INDEX = nearestRayPresetIndex(80)

01239 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function getBaseEffectiveRayPresetIndex(baseIdx)
01240 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local n = (RAY_PRESETS and #RAY_PRESETS) or 0
01241 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if n <= 0 then return 1 end
01242 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local idx = clampInt(baseIdx or (RAY_PRESET_INDEX or 1), 1, n)
01243 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     -- WALL RES mode should always impact rendering quality/perf.
01244 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     -- FAST mode biases one preset step lower (fewer rays / wider columns).
01245 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if LOW_RES_WALLS and LOW_RES_MODE == "fast" and idx > 1 then
01246 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         idx = idx - 1
01247 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01248 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return idx
01249 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end

01395 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] function getClassDefById(classId)
01396 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local fallbackId = CLASS_FALLBACK_ORDER[1] or "warrior"
01397 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if getGameClass then
01398 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local classDef = getGameClass(classId or fallbackId)
01399 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if classDef and classDef.id then
01400 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             return classDef
01401 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
01402 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01403 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local id = classId or fallbackId
01404 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not CLASS_FALLBACKS[id] then
01405 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         id = fallbackId
01406 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01407 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return CLASS_FALLBACKS[id]
01408 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end

01413 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01414 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return CLASS_FALLBACK_ORDER

01471 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] function getClassSelectionIndexForId(classId)
01472 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local order = getClassOrder()
01473 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local normalized = sanitizeClassId(classId)
01474 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     for i = 1, #order do
01475 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if order[i] == normalized then
01476 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             return i
01477 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
01478 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01479 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return 1
01480 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end
01481 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
01482 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] function getClassIdForSelection(index)
01483 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local order = getClassOrder()
01484 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local count = #order
01485 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if count <= 0 then
01486 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return "warrior", 1, 1
01487 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01488 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local idx = math.floor(index or 1)
01489 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if idx < 1 then idx = count end
01490 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if idx > count then idx = 1 end
01491 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return order[idx], idx, count
01492 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end

01494 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] function toNumber(value, fallback)
01495 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local n = tonumber(value)
01496 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if n == nil then
01497 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return fallback
01498 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01499 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return n
01500 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end

01505 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return out
01506 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01507 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local text = tostring(input)
01508 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local sep = separator or ","
01509 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if sep == "" then
01510 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         out[1] = text
01511 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return out
01512 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01513 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local start = 1
01514 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     while true do
01515 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local idx = string.find(text, sep, start, true)
01516 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if not idx then
01517 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             out[#out + 1] = string.sub(text, start)
01518 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             break
01519 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
01520 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         out[#out + 1] = string.sub(text, start, idx - 1)
01521 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         start = idx + #sep
01522 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01523 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return out
01524 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end
01525 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
01526 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] function sanitizeSaveToken(value)
01527 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local text = tostring(value or "")
01528 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     text = string.gsub(text, "\r", "")
01529 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     text = string.gsub(text, "\n", "")
01530 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     text = string.gsub(text, "|", "")
01531 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return text
01532 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end

01552 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local src = slot or makeEmptySaveSlot(1)
01553 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return {
01554 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         slot = src.slot,

01564 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         enemy_state = src.enemy_state,
01565 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         potion_state = src.potion_state,

01569 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] function normalizeSaveSlots()
01570 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     for i = 1, SAVE_SLOT_COUNT do
01571 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local slot = saveSlots[i]
01572 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if not slot then
01573 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             slot = makeEmptySaveSlot(i)
01574 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         else
01575 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             slot = copySaveSlot(slot)
01576 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             slot.slot = i
01577 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             slot.used = slot.used and true or false
01578 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             slot.level_id = math.floor(toNumber(slot.level_id, 1))
01579 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if not LEVELS[slot.level_id] then
01580 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 slot.level_id = 1
01581 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             end
01582 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             slot.class_id = sanitizeClassId(slot.class_id)
01583 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             slot.player_x = toNumber(slot.player_x, 2.5)
01584 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             slot.player_y = toNumber(slot.player_y, 2.5)
01585 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             slot.player_dir = math.floor(toNumber(slot.player_dir, 0)) % 64
01586 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             slot.player_health = math.floor(toNumber(slot.player_health, MAX_HEALTH or 100))
01587 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if slot.player_health < 1 then slot.player_health = 1 end
01588 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if slot.player_health > (MAX_HEALTH or 100) then slot.player_health = (MAX_HEALTH or 100) end
01589 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             slot.soldiers_killed = math.floor(toNumber(slot.soldiers_killed, 0))
01590 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if slot.soldiers_killed < 0 then slot.soldiers_killed = 0 end
01591 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             slot.total_soldiers = math.floor(toNumber(slot.total_soldiers, 0))
01592 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if slot.total_soldiers < 0 then slot.total_soldiers = 0 end
01593 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             slot.enemy_state = tostring(slot.enemy_state or "")
01594 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             slot.potion_state = tostring(slot.potion_state or "")
01595 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
01596 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         saveSlots[i] = slot
01597 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01598 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end
01599 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
01600 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] function serializeSaveSlots()
01601 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     normalizeSaveSlots()
01602 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local lines = {SAVE_FILE_HEADER}
01603 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     for i = 1, SAVE_SLOT_COUNT do
01604 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local slot = saveSlots[i] or makeEmptySaveSlot(i)
01605 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         lines[#lines + 1] = table.concat({
01606 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             tostring(i),
01607 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             slot.used and "1" or "0",
01608 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             tostring(slot.level_id or 1),
01609 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             sanitizeSaveToken(slot.class_id or "warrior"),
01610 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             string.format("%.4f", toNumber(slot.player_x, 2.5)),
01611 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             string.format("%.4f", toNumber(slot.player_y, 2.5)),
01612 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             tostring(math.floor(toNumber(slot.player_dir, 0)) % 64),
01613 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             tostring(math.floor(toNumber(slot.player_health, MAX_HEALTH or 100))),
01614 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             tostring(math.floor(toNumber(slot.soldiers_killed, 0))),
01615 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             tostring(math.floor(toNumber(slot.total_soldiers, 0))),
01616 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             sanitizeSaveToken(slot.enemy_state or ""),
01617 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             sanitizeSaveToken(slot.potion_state or ""),
01618 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         }, "|")
01619 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01620 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return table.concat(lines, "\n")
01621 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end

01623 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] function deserializeSaveSlots(payload)
01624 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not payload or payload == "" then
01625 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return false, "empty_payload"
01626 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01627 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
01628 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local normalized = string.gsub(tostring(payload), "\r", "")
01629 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local lines = {}
01630 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     for line in string.gmatch(normalized, "([^\n]+)") do
01631 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if line and line ~= "" then
01632 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             lines[#lines + 1] = line
01633 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
01634 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01635 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if #lines == 0 then
01636 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return false, "empty_lines"
01637 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01638 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if lines[1] ~= SAVE_FILE_HEADER then
01639 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return false, "invalid_header"
01640 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01641 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
01642 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     saveSlots = {}
01643 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     for i = 2, #lines do
01644 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local parts = splitByPlain(lines[i], "|")
01645 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if #parts >= 12 then
01646 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local slotIndex = math.floor(toNumber(parts[1], 0))
01647 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if slotIndex >= 1 and slotIndex <= SAVE_SLOT_COUNT then
01648 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 saveSlots[slotIndex] = {
01649 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     slot = slotIndex,
01650 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     used = (toNumber(parts[2], 0) ~= 0),
01651 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     level_id = math.floor(toNumber(parts[3], 1)),
01652 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     class_id = sanitizeClassId(parts[4]),
01653 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     player_x = toNumber(parts[5], 2.5),
01654 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     player_y = toNumber(parts[6], 2.5),
01655 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     player_dir = math.floor(toNumber(parts[7], 0)) % 64,
01656 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     player_health = math.floor(toNumber(parts[8], MAX_HEALTH or 100)),
01657 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     soldiers_killed = math.floor(toNumber(parts[9], 0)),
01658 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     total_soldiers = math.floor(toNumber(parts[10], 0)),
01659 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     enemy_state = parts[11] or "",
01660 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     potion_state = parts[12] or "",
01661 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 }
01662 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             end
01663 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
01664 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01665 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
01666 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     normalizeSaveSlots()
01667 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return true, nil
01668 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end

01671 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return vmupro and vmupro.file and vmupro.file.read and vmupro.file.write
01672 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end

01674 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] function writeSaveSlotsToDisk()
01675 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     normalizeSaveSlots()
01676 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not hasFileApi() then
01677 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return false, "file_api_unavailable"
01678 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01679 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
01680 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if vmupro.file.folderExists and vmupro.file.createFolder then
01681 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if not vmupro.file.folderExists("/sdcard/inner_sanctum") then
01682 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local created = vmupro.file.createFolder("/sdcard/inner_sanctum")
01683 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if not created then
01684 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 return false, "create_folder_failed"
01685 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             end
01686 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
01687 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01688 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
01689 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if vmupro.file.exists and vmupro.file.createFile and (not vmupro.file.exists(SAVE_FILE_PATH)) then
01690 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         vmupro.file.createFile(SAVE_FILE_PATH)
01691 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01692 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
01693 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local encoded = serializeSaveSlots()
01694 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local okWrite = vmupro.file.write(SAVE_FILE_PATH, encoded)
01695 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not okWrite then
01696 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return false, "write_failed"
01697 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01698 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return true, nil
01699 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end

01701 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] function loadSaveSlotsFromDisk()
01702 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     normalizeSaveSlots()
01703 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not hasFileApi() then
01704 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return false, "file_api_unavailable"
01705 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01706 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if vmupro.file.exists and (not vmupro.file.exists(SAVE_FILE_PATH)) then
01707 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return false, "missing_file"

01711 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return false, "read_failed"
01712 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01713 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return deserializeSaveSlots(payload)
01714 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end

01716 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] function getSaveSlotSummary(slotIndex)
01717 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     normalizeSaveSlots()
01718 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local idx = math.floor(toNumber(slotIndex, 1))
01719 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if idx < 1 then idx = 1 end
01720 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if idx > SAVE_SLOT_COUNT then idx = SAVE_SLOT_COUNT end
01721 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local slot = saveSlots[idx] or makeEmptySaveSlot(idx)
01722 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not slot.used then
01723 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return "SLOT " .. tostring(idx), "EMPTY"
01724 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01725 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local levelLabel = getLevelLabel(slot.level_id or 1)
01726 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local classLabel = string.upper(getClassName(slot.class_id))
01727 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return "SLOT " .. tostring(idx), "LEVEL " .. tostring(levelLabel) .. "  " .. classLabel
01728 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end

01730 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] function countEnemiesInSprites()
01731 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not sprites then return 0 end
01732 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local total = 0
01733 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     for i = 1, #sprites do
01734 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local s = sprites[i]
01735 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if s and isEnemyType(s.t) then
01736 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             total = total + 1
01737 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
01738 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01739 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return total
01740 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end

01742 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] function countDeadEnemiesInSprites()
01743 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not sprites then return 0 end
01744 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local total = 0
01745 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     for i = 1, #sprites do

01750 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01751 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return total

01754 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] function buildEnemyStateSnapshot()
01755 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not sprites then
01756 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return ""
01757 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01758 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local entries = {}
01759 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     for i = 1, #sprites do
01760 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local s = sprites[i]
01761 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if s and isEnemyType(s.t) then
01762 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local alive = 1
01763 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if s.alive == false or s.dead == true then
01764 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 alive = 0
01765 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             end
01766 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local hp = math.floor(toNumber(s.hp, ENEMY_MAX_HP))
01767 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if hp < 0 then hp = 0 end
01768 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             entries[#entries + 1] = tostring(alive) .. ":" .. tostring(hp)
01769 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
01770 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01771 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return table.concat(entries, ";")
01772 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end
01773 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
01774 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] function buildPotionStateSnapshot()
01775 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not sprites then
01776 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return ""
01777 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01778 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local entries = {}
01779 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     for i = 1, #sprites do
01780 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local s = sprites[i]
01781 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if s and s.t == 7 then
01782 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             entries[#entries + 1] = s.collected and "1" or "0"
01783 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
01784 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01785 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return table.concat(entries, ";")
01786 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end
01787 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
01788 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] function applyEnemyStateSnapshot(snapshot)
01789 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not sprites then
01790 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return 0
01791 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01792 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local entries = splitByPlain(snapshot or "", ";")
01793 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local enemyIdx = 1
01794 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local deadCount = 0
01795 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     for i = 1, #sprites do
01796 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local s = sprites[i]
01797 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if s and isEnemyType(s.t) then
01798 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local entry = entries[enemyIdx] or ""
01799 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if entry ~= "" then
01800 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 local pair = splitByPlain(entry, ":")
01801 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 local aliveFlag = toNumber(pair[1], 1)
01802 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 local hpValue = math.floor(toNumber(pair[2], s.hp or ENEMY_MAX_HP))
01803 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 if hpValue < 0 then hpValue = 0 end
01804 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 if hpValue > 300 then hpValue = 300 end
01805 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 if aliveFlag ~= 0 and hpValue > 0 then
01806 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     s.alive = true
01807 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     s.dead = false
01808 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     s.dying = false
01809 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     s.hp = hpValue
01810 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 else
01811 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     s.alive = false
01812 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     s.dead = true
01813 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     s.dying = false
01814 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     s.hp = 0
01815 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     deadCount = deadCount + 1
01816 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 end
01817 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 s.attackAnim = 0
01818 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 s.attackFrame = 1
01819 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 s.attackDidHit = false
01820 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 s.state = nil
01821 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 s.deathFrame = nil
01822 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 s.deathTick = nil
01823 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             elseif s.alive == false or s.dead == true then
01824 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 deadCount = deadCount + 1
01825 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             end
01826 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             enemyIdx = enemyIdx + 1
01827 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
01828 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01829 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return deadCount
01830 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end

01832 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] function applyPotionStateSnapshot(snapshot)
01833 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not sprites then
01834 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return
01835 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01836 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local entries = splitByPlain(snapshot or "", ";")
01837 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local potionIdx = 1

01839 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local s = sprites[i]

01842 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if entry ~= "" then

01850 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] function captureCurrentSaveSlot(slotIndex)
01851 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local slot = makeEmptySaveSlot(slotIndex)
01852 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     slot.used = true
01853 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     slot.level_id = currentLevel or 1
01854 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not LEVELS[slot.level_id] then
01855 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         slot.level_id = 1
01856 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01857 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     slot.class_id = getCurrentClassId()
01858 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     slot.player_x = toNumber(px, 2.5)
01859 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     slot.player_y = toNumber(py, 2.5)
01860 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     slot.player_dir = math.floor(toNumber(pdir, 0)) % 64
01861 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     slot.player_health = math.floor(toNumber(playerHealth, MAX_HEALTH or 100))
01862 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if slot.player_health < 1 then slot.player_health = 1 end
01863 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if slot.player_health > (MAX_HEALTH or 100) then slot.player_health = (MAX_HEALTH or 100) end
01864 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     slot.enemy_state = buildEnemyStateSnapshot()
01865 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     slot.potion_state = buildPotionStateSnapshot()
01866 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     slot.total_soldiers = countEnemiesInSprites()
01867 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local observedKilled = countDeadEnemiesInSprites()
01868 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local trackedKilled = math.floor(toNumber(soldiersKilled, 0))
01869 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if trackedKilled < observedKilled then
01870 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         trackedKilled = observedKilled
01871 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01872 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if trackedKilled < 0 then trackedKilled = 0 end
01873 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if trackedKilled > slot.total_soldiers then trackedKilled = slot.total_soldiers end
01874 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     slot.soldiers_killed = trackedKilled
01875 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return slot
01876 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end

01881 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return false, "invalid_slot"
01882 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01883 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     normalizeSaveSlots()

01885 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local okWrite, errWrite = writeSaveSlotsToDisk()
01886 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not okWrite and errWrite ~= "file_api_unavailable" then
01887 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return false, errWrite
01888 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01889 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return true, nil
01890 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end

01935 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]

01988 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function deepCopy(value)
01989 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if type(value) ~= "table" then
01990 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return value
01991 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
01992 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local out = {}
01993 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local len = #value
01994 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if len > 0 then
01995 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         for i = 1, len do
01996 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             out[i] = deepCopy(value[i])
01997 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
01998 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         for k, v in pairs(value) do
01999 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if type(k) ~= "number" then
02000 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 out[k] = deepCopy(v)
02001 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             end
02002 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
02003 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     else
02004 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         for k, v in pairs(value) do
02005 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             out[k] = deepCopy(v)
02006 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
02007 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
02008 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return out
02009 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end
02010 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
02011 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function countEnemies(spriteList)
02012 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local count = 0
02013 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     for i = 1, #spriteList do
02014 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local s = spriteList[i]
02015 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if s.t == 5 or s.t == 6 then
02016 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             count = count + 1
02017 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
02018 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
02019 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return count
02020 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end
02021 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
02022 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function countAdjacentOpenTiles(sourceMap, mx, my)
02023 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local function tileAt(tx, ty)
02024 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if tx < 0 or tx > 15 or ty < 0 or ty > 15 then
02025 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             return 1
02026 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
02027 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local row = sourceMap[ty + 1]
02028 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if not row then return 1 end
02029 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return row[tx + 1] or 1
02030 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
02031 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local openCount = 0
02032 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if tileAt(mx, my - 1) == 0 then openCount = openCount + 1 end
02033 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if tileAt(mx, my + 1) == 0 then openCount = openCount + 1 end
02034 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if tileAt(mx - 1, my) == 0 then openCount = openCount + 1 end
02035 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if tileAt(mx + 1, my) == 0 then openCount = openCount + 1 end
02036 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return openCount
02037 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end
02038 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
02039 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function wallVariantHash(mx, my, levelId, salt)
02040 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local v = (((mx + 1) * 1973) + ((my + 1) * 9277) + ((levelId or 1) * 2663) + ((salt or 0) * 811)) % 104729
02041 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     v = ((v * 131) + 907) % 104729
02042 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return v
02043 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end
02044 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
02045 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function chooseWallVariant(mx, my, levelId, sourceMap)
02046 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     -- Deterministic wall variety (no math.random crash risk).
02047 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local openCount = countAdjacentOpenTiles(sourceMap, mx, my)
02048 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local isDeadEndCap = (openCount == 1)
02049 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
02050 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     -- Keep decorative types 5/6 rare so they don't feel deceptive in navigation.
02051 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local accentRatePerThousand = isDeadEndCap and 55 or 12 -- 5.5% dead-ends, 1.2% elsewhere
02052 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local accentRoll = wallVariantHash(mx, my, levelId, 1) % 1000
02053 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if accentRoll < accentRatePerThousand then
02054 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local accentPick = wallVariantHash(mx, my, levelId, 2) % 100
02055 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if accentPick < 72 then
02056 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             return 5 -- diamond accent
02057 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
02058 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return 6 -- window accent (rarer)
02059 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
02060 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
02061 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     -- Primary walls (1-4) get broad, deterministic variety for immersion.
02062 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local bucket = wallVariantHash(mx, my, levelId, 3) % 100
02063 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if bucket < 30 then return 1 end
02064 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if bucket < 57 then return 2 end
02065 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if bucket < 80 then return 3 end
02066 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return 4
02067 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end

02069 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function loadLevel(levelId)
02070 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local level = LEVELS[levelId]
02071 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not level then return end
02072 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     currentLevel = levelId
02073 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if level.perfDisableEnemies ~= nil then
02074 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         DEBUG_DISABLE_ENEMIES = level.perfDisableEnemies
02075 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
02076 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if level.perfDisableTextures ~= nil then
02077 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         DEBUG_DISABLE_WALL_TEXTURE = level.perfDisableTextures
02078 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
02079 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if level.perfDisableProps ~= nil then
02080 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         DEBUG_DISABLE_PROPS = level.perfDisableProps
02081 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
02082 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if type(level.name) == "string" and level.name:sub(1, 2) == "p-" then
02083 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         enableBootLogs = false
02084 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         DEBUG_WALL_QUADS_LOG = false
02085 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
02086 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     map = deepCopy(level.map)
02087 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     for my = 0, 15 do
02088 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local row = map[my + 1]
02089 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if row then
02090 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             for mx = 0, 15 do
02091 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 if row[mx + 1] and row[mx + 1] > 0 then
02092 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     row[mx + 1] = chooseWallVariant(mx, my, levelId, map)
02093 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 end
02094 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             end
02095 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
02096 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
02097 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     sprites = deepCopy(level.sprites)
02098 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local function isOpenFloor(mx, my)
02099 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if mx < 1 or mx > 14 or my < 1 or my > 14 then return false end
02100 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if map[my + 1][mx + 1] ~= 0 then return false end
02101 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if map[my + 1][mx] ~= 0 then return false end
02102 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if map[my + 1][mx + 2] ~= 0 then return false end
02103 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if map[my][mx + 1] ~= 0 then return false end
02104 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if map[my + 2][mx + 1] ~= 0 then return false end
02105 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return true
02106 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
02107 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local function tileAt(mx, my)
02108 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if mx < 0 or mx > 15 or my < 0 or my > 15 then
02109 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             return 1
02110 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
02111 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return map[my + 1][mx + 1] or 1
02112 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
02113 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local function isDoorwayTile(mx, my)
02114 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local n = tileAt(mx, my - 1) > 0
02115 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local s = tileAt(mx, my + 1) > 0
02116 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local w = tileAt(mx - 1, my) > 0
02117 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local e = tileAt(mx + 1, my) > 0
02118 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return (n and s and not e and not w) or (e and w and not n and not s)
02119 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
02120 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local function isWallAttached(mx, my)
02121 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if tileAt(mx, my) ~= 0 then return false end
02122 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local n = tileAt(mx, my - 1) > 0
02123 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local s = tileAt(mx, my + 1) > 0
02124 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local w = tileAt(mx - 1, my) > 0
02125 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local e = tileAt(mx + 1, my) > 0
02126 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if isDoorwayTile(mx, my) then return false end
02127 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         -- Require a nearby wall, but avoid pure hallway gaps
02128 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if (n and s and not e and not w) or (e and w and not n and not s) then
02129 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             return false
02130 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
02131 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return n or s or w or e
02132 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
02133 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if sprites then
02134 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local filteredFloor = {}
02135 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         for i = 1, #sprites do
02136 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local s = sprites[i]
02137 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if s and (s.t == 1 or s.t == 2 or s.t == 3 or s.t == 4) then
02138 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 local mx = math.floor(s.x)
02139 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 local my = math.floor(s.y)
02140 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 if isWallAttached(mx, my) then
02141 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     filteredFloor[#filteredFloor + 1] = s
02142 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 end
02143 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             elseif s and (s.t == 7 or s.t == 8) then
02144 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 local mx = math.floor(s.x)
02145 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 local my = math.floor(s.y)
02146 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 if isOpenFloor(mx, my) then
02147 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     filteredFloor[#filteredFloor + 1] = s
02148 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 end
02149 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             else
02150 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 filteredFloor[#filteredFloor + 1] = s
02151 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             end
02152 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
02153 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         sprites = filteredFloor
02154 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
02155 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if DEBUG_DISABLE_PROPS then
02156 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local filtered = {}
02157 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         for i = 1, #sprites do
02158 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local s = sprites[i]
02159 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if s.t == 7 or not isPropType(s.t) then
02160 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 filtered[#filtered + 1] = s
02161 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             end
02162 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
02163 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         sprites = filtered
02164 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
02165 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     totalSoldiers = countEnemies(sprites)
02166 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     px = level.playerStart.x
02167 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     py = level.playerStart.y
02168 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     pdir = level.playerStart.dir
02169 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     lastSafeWallX = px
02170 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     lastSafeWallY = py
02171 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end

02300 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function loadTextureSheetWithValidation(path, textureName)
02301 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local success, sheet = pcall(function()
02302 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return vmupro.sprite.newSheet(path)
02303 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end)
02304 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
02305 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not success then
02306 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         safeLog("ERROR", string.format(
02307 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             "Failed to load texture sheet '%s' from path: %s. Error: %s",
02308 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             textureName, path, tostring(sheet)
02309 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         ))
02310 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return nil
02311 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
02312 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
02313 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not sheet then
02314 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         safeLog("ERROR", string.format(
02315 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             "Texture sheet '%s' returned nil from path: %s",
02316 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             textureName, path
02317 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         ))
02318 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return nil
02319 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
02320 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
02321 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local frameCount = sheet.frameCount or 0
02322 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local frameWidth = sheet.frameWidth or 0
02323 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local frameHeight = sheet.frameHeight or 0
02324 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if frameCount <= 0 or frameWidth <= 0 or frameHeight <= 0 then
02325 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         safeLog("ERROR", string.format(
02326 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             "Texture sheet '%s' has invalid frame metadata: count=%s frame=%sx%s path=%s",
02327 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             textureName, tostring(frameCount), tostring(frameWidth), tostring(frameHeight), path
02328 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         ))
02329 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return nil
02330 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
02331 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
02332 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if frameWidth ~= 1 or frameHeight ~= 128 then
02333 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         safeLog("ERROR", string.format(
02334 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             "Texture sheet '%s' has unexpected frame size %dx%d (expected 1x128): %s",
02335 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             textureName, frameWidth, frameHeight, path
02336 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         ))
02337 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return nil
02338 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
02339 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
02340 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if frameCount < 64 then
02341 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         safeLog("ERROR", string.format(
02342 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             "Texture sheet '%s' has too few frames: count=%d path=%s",
02343 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             textureName, frameCount, path
02344 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         ))
02345 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return nil
02346 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
02347 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
02348 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     safeLog("INFO", string.format(
02349 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         "Texture sheet '%s' loaded: frame %dx%d, count=%d, transparentColor=0x%04X (column path)",
02350 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         textureName, frameWidth, frameHeight, frameCount, sheet.transparentColor or 0
02351 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     ))
02352 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return sheet
02353 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end

02355 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function getWall1VariantConfig()
02356 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local variants = WALL1_FORMAT_VARIANTS or {}
02357 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local n = #variants
02358 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if n <= 0 then
02359 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return {label = "PNG16", base = "sprites/wall_textures/wall-1-tile", sheet = "sprites/wall_textures/wall-1-tile-table-1-128"}
02360 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
02361 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     WALL1_FORMAT_INDEX = clampInt(WALL1_FORMAT_INDEX or 1, 1, n)
02362 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return variants[WALL1_FORMAT_INDEX] or variants[1]
02363 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end

02394 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] function loadWallTextures()
02395 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if wallTextureLoadAttempted then return end
02396 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     wallTextureLoadAttempted = true
02397 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local wall1Cfg = getWall1VariantConfig()
02398 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local wall1BasePath = wall1Cfg.base or "sprites/wall_textures/wall-1-tile"
02399 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local wall1SheetPath = wall1Cfg.sheet or "sprites/wall_textures/wall-1-tile-table-1-128"
02400 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     safeLog("INFO", string.format(
02401 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         "[TEX] wall1 variant=%s base=%s sheet=%s wallKey=%s colorKeyOverride=%s",

02405 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         getWallKeyModeLabel(),
02406 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         WALL_FORCE_COLORKEY_OVERRIDE and "ON" or "OFF"
02407 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     ))
02408 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     -- Base textures (your selected names).
02409 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     wallStone = loadTextureWithValidation(wall1BasePath, "wall_1")
02410 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     wallBrick = loadTextureWithValidation("sprites/wall_textures/wall-2-tile", "wall_2")
02411 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     wallMoss = loadTextureWithValidation("sprites/wall_textures/wall-3-tile", "wall_3")
02412 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     wallMetal = loadTextureWithValidation("sprites/wall_textures/wall-4-tile", "wall_4")
02413 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     wallWood = loadTextureWithValidation("sprites/wall_textures/Wall-Diamond-Tile", "wall_diamond")

02415 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]

02423 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     forceWallTextureColorKeys()
02424 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]
