04745 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
04746 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     -- Mip tiers quantize texture-column selection for stable far detail and lower aliasing.
04747 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     -- MIP1 uses stride-only LOD (no texel quantization) to avoid near-distance angle shimmer.
04748 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local mip = mipLevel or 0
04749 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if mip > 1 then

04751 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if mip >= 4 then
04752 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             groupSize = 6
04753 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         elseif mip == 3 then
04754 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             groupSize = 4
04755 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         elseif mip == 2 then
04756 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             groupSize = 3
04757 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
04758 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if groupSize > 1 and frameCount > groupSize then
04759 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             frameIndex = (math.floor((frameIndex - 1) / groupSize) * groupSize) + 1
04760 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if frameIndex ~= frameIndex or frameIndex == math.huge or frameIndex == -math.huge then
04761 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 frameIndex = 1
04762 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             end
04763 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if frameIndex > frameCount then frameIndex = frameCount end
04764 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end

04766 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]

04770 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if distToWall and distToWall <= seamNearDist then
04771 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         allowSeamOverdraw = false
04772 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
04773 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if allowSeamOverdraw and drawWidth <= 4 then

04779 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if seamPx > roomRight then seamPx = roomRight end

04781 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
04782 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
04783 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]

04795 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end

04804 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if x2 > 239 then x2 = 239 end

04855 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function ensureExpTables()
04856 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if expTablesReady then return end
04857 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local dirSteps = EXP_FIXED_DIR_STEPS or 2048
04858 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local twoPi = (renderCfg and renderCfg.twoPi) or 6.28318
04859 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     for i = 0, dirSteps - 1 do
04860 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local angle = (i * twoPi) / dirSteps
04861 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local cx = math.cos(angle)
04862 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local sy = math.sin(angle)
04863 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         rayDirCos[i] = cx
04864 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         rayDirSin[i] = sy
04865 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         rayDirXFix[i] = math.floor(cx * 256)
04866 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         rayDirYFix[i] = math.floor(sy * 256)
04867 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if math.abs(cx) < 0.0000001 then
04868 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             invRayDirXFix[i] = 0x7FFFFFFF
04869 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         else
04870 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             invRayDirXFix[i] = math.floor((1 / cx) * 65536)
04871 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
04872 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if math.abs(sy) < 0.0000001 then
04873 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             invRayDirYFix[i] = 0x7FFFFFFF
04874 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         else
04875 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             invRayDirYFix[i] = math.floor((1 / sy) * 65536)
04876 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
04877 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         deltaDistXFix[i] = math.abs(invRayDirXFix[i])
04878 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         deltaDistYFix[i] = math.abs(invRayDirYFix[i])
04879 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
04880 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     expTablesReady = true
04881 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end
04882 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
04883 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function ensureExpHeightLut()
04884 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if expHeightLutReady then return end
04885 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local wallScale = VIEWPORT_H - 20
04886 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local size = EXP_DIST_LUT_SIZE or 256
04887 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local maxDist = EXP_MAX_DIST or 16
04888 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     for i = 1, size do
04889 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local dist = (i / size) * maxDist
04890 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if dist < 0.4 then dist = 0.4 end
04891 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         expHeightLut[i] = math.floor(wallScale / dist)
04892 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
04893 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     for h = 0, VIEWPORT_H do
04894 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         expScaleYLut[h] = h / 128
04895 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
04896 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     expHeightLutReady = true
04897 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end
04898 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
04899 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function getExpRayOffsets(rayCols)
04900 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local key = tostring(rayCols)
04901 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local cached = expRayOffsets[key]
04902 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if cached then return cached end
04903 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local offsets = {}
04904 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if rayCols <= 1 then
04905 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         offsets[1] = 0
04906 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     else
04907 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local subdiv = EXP_FIXED_DIR_SUBDIV or 32
04908 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local fovUnits = (renderCfg.fovSteps or 9) * subdiv
04909 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local half = fovUnits / 2
04910 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         for x = 0, rayCols - 1 do
04911 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local t = x / (rayCols - 1)
04912 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local off = -half + t * fovUnits
04913 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if off >= 0 then
04914 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 offsets[x + 1] = math.floor(off + 0.5)
04915 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             else
04916 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 offsets[x + 1] = math.ceil(off - 0.5)
04917 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             end
04918 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
04919 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
04920 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     expRayOffsets[key] = offsets
04921 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return offsets
04922 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end
04923 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
04924 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function getStartSolidRayFallback(pxVal, pyVal, mapX, mapY, startTile)
04925 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local fx = pxVal - mapX
04926 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local fy = pyVal - mapY
04927 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if fx < 0 then fx = 0 elseif fx > 0.999 then fx = 0.999 end
04928 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if fy < 0 then fy = 0 elseif fy > 0.999 then fy = 0.999 end
04929 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
04930 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local best = fx
04931 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local side = 0
04932 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local texCoord = fy
04933 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
04934 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local rightDist = 1.0 - fx
04935 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if rightDist < best then
04936 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         best = rightDist
04937 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         side = 0
04938 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         texCoord = fy
04939 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
04940 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
04941 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local topDist = fy
04942 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if topDist < best then
04943 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         best = topDist
04944 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         side = 1
04945 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         texCoord = fx
04946 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
04947 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
04948 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local bottomDist = 1.0 - fy
04949 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if bottomDist < best then
04950 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         side = 1
04951 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         texCoord = fx
04952 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
04953 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
04954 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if texCoord < 0.001 then texCoord = 0.001 end
04955 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if texCoord > 0.998 then texCoord = 0.998 end
04956 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     PERF_MONITOR_RAY_START_SOLID = (PERF_MONITOR_RAY_START_SOLID or 0) + 1
04957 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return getPlayerRenderNearClipDist(), startTile, side, texCoord, true
04958 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end
04959 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
04960 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function expCastRayFixed(rayDir, maxDist)
04961 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     ensureExpTables()
04962 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local posXFix = math.floor(px * EXP_FIX_TILE)
04963 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local posYFix = math.floor(py * EXP_FIX_TILE)
04964 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local mapX = math.floor(posXFix / EXP_FIX_TILE)
04965 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local mapY = math.floor(posYFix / EXP_FIX_TILE)
04966 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local rayMaxDist = maxDist or 16
04967 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if rayMaxDist < 0.25 then
04968 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         rayMaxDist = 0.25
04969 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
04970 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local rayMaxDistFix = math.floor(rayMaxDist * EXP_FIX_DIST)
04971 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
04972 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     -- Guard against rare movement penetration: stabilize rendering when inside a wall cell.
04973 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if mapX >= 0 and mapX < 16 and mapY >= 0 and mapY < 16 then
04974 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local startTile = map and map[mapY + 1] and map[mapY + 1][mapX + 1] or 0
04975 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if startTile and startTile > 0 then
04976 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             return getStartSolidRayFallback(px, py, mapX, mapY, startTile)
04977 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
04978 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
04979 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
04980 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local dirXFix = rayDirXFix[rayDir] or 0
04981 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local dirYFix = rayDirYFix[rayDir] or 0
04982 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local stepX = (dirXFix < 0) and -1 or 1
04983 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local stepY = (dirYFix < 0) and -1 or 1
04984 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
04985 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local deltaX = deltaDistXFix[rayDir] or 0x7FFFFFFF
04986 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local deltaY = deltaDistYFix[rayDir] or 0x7FFFFFFF
04987 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
04988 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local nextXFix = (mapX + (stepX > 0 and 1 or 0)) * EXP_FIX_TILE
04989 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local nextYFix = (mapY + (stepY > 0 and 1 or 0)) * EXP_FIX_TILE
04990 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local distToNextX = nextXFix - posXFix
04991 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local distToNextY = nextYFix - posYFix
04992 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if distToNextX < 0 then distToNextX = -distToNextX end
04993 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if distToNextY < 0 then distToNextY = -distToNextY end
04994 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
04995 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local sideDistX = math.floor((distToNextX * deltaX) / EXP_FIX_TILE)
04996 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local sideDistY = math.floor((distToNextY * deltaY) / EXP_FIX_TILE)
04997 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
04998 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local side = 0
04999 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local wtype = 1
05000 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local hit = false
05001 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local maxSteps = EXP_MAX_STEPS or 8
05002 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     for _ = 1, maxSteps do
05003 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local nextDist = sideDistX
05004 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if sideDistY < nextDist then nextDist = sideDistY end
05005 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if nextDist > rayMaxDistFix then
05006 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             break
05007 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
05008 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if sideDistX < sideDistY then
05009 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             sideDistX = sideDistX + deltaX
05010 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             mapX = mapX + stepX
05011 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             side = 0
05012 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         else
05013 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             sideDistY = sideDistY + deltaY
05014 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             mapY = mapY + stepY
05015 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             side = 1
05016 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
05017 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if mapX < 0 or mapX >= 16 or mapY < 0 or mapY >= 16 then
05018 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             break
05019 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
05020 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         wtype = map[mapY + 1][mapX + 1]
05021 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if wtype > 0 then
05022 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             hit = true
05023 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             break
05024 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
05025 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
05026 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not hit then
05027 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return rayMaxDist, 1, 0, 0, false
05028 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
05029 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
05030 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local perpFix
05031 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if side == 0 then
05032 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local numFix = ((mapX * EXP_FIX_TILE) - posXFix + ((stepX == -1) and EXP_FIX_TILE or 0))
05033 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         perpFix = math.floor((numFix * (invRayDirXFix[rayDir] or 0)) / EXP_FIX_TILE)
05034 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     else
05035 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local numFix = ((mapY * EXP_FIX_TILE) - posYFix + ((stepY == -1) and EXP_FIX_TILE or 0))
05036 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         perpFix = math.floor((numFix * (invRayDirYFix[rayDir] or 0)) / EXP_FIX_TILE)
05037 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
05038 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if perpFix < 1 then perpFix = 1 end
05039 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
05040 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local texFix
05041 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if side == 0 then
05042 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local texCalc = posYFix + math.floor((perpFix * dirYFix) / EXP_FIX_DIST)
05043 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         texFix = texCalc % EXP_FIX_TILE
05044 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     else
05045 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local texCalc = posXFix + math.floor((perpFix * dirXFix) / EXP_FIX_DIST)
05046 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         texFix = texCalc % EXP_FIX_TILE
05047 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
05048 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local texCoord = texFix / EXP_FIX_TILE
05049 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local dist = perpFix / EXP_FIX_DIST
05050 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if dist > rayMaxDist then
05051 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return rayMaxDist, 1, 0, 0, false
05052 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
05053 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return dist, wtype, side, texCoord, true
05054 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end
05055 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
05056 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local expDepthBuf = {}
05057 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function renderWallsExperimentalHybrid()
05058 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     -- Stability-first EXP-H: use one raycast projection model at all distances.
05059 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     -- This prevents wall seams/shape shifts when draw distance changes.
05060 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local hybridViewDist = EXP_VIEW_DIST or (EXP_TEX_MAX_DIST or 8.0)
05061 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local texView = EXP_TEX_MAX_DIST or hybridViewDist
05062 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local fogView = FOG_END or texView
05063 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if fogView < 0.5 then fogView = 0.5 end
05064 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local rayTraceDist = texView
05065 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if rayTraceDist < 0.5 then rayTraceDist = 0.5 end
05066 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
05067 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local fovRad = renderCfg.fovSteps * (renderCfg.twoPi / 64)
05068 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local playerDir = pdir % 64
05069 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local playerAngle = playerDir * (renderCfg.twoPi / 64)
05070 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local playerCos = math.cos(playerAngle)
05071 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local playerSin = math.sin(playerAngle)
05072 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local rayCols = 60
05073 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local colW = 4
05074 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local basePresetIdx = RAY_PRESET_INDEX or 1
05075 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local effectivePresetIdx = getEffectiveRayPresetIndex(basePresetIdx)
05076 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local preset = RAY_PRESETS and RAY_PRESETS[effectivePresetIdx] or nil
05077 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if preset then
05078 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         rayCols = preset.rays or rayCols
05079 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         colW = preset.colW or colW
05080 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     elseif LOW_RES_WALLS then
05081 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if LOW_RES_MODE == "fast" then
05082 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             rayCols = 40
05083 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             colW = 6
05084 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         else
05085 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             rayCols = 60
05086 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             colW = 4
05087 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
05088 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
05089 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local useFixedRaycast = (USE_FIXED_RAYCAST == true) and (DEBUG_FORCE_FLOAT_RAYCAST ~= true)
05090 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local perfSample = (DEBUG_PERF_MONITOR == true) and (PERF_MONITOR_ACTIVE_SAMPLE == true)
05091 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local trackCounters = (DEBUG_PERF_MONITOR == true)
05092 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local canTime = perfSample and vmupro and vmupro.system and vmupro.system.getTimeUs
05093 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local rayOffsets = nil
05094 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local playerDirFix = 0
05095 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local rayStep = 0
05096 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local stepCos1, stepCos2, stepCos3, stepCos4
05097 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local stepSin1, stepSin2, stepSin3, stepSin4
05098 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local rayCos = 0
05099 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local raySin = 0
05100 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if useFixedRaycast then
05101 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         ensureExpTables()
05102 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         playerDirFix = (playerDir % 64) * (EXP_FIXED_DIR_SUBDIV or 32)
05103 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         rayOffsets = getExpRayOffsets(rayCols)
05104 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     else
05105 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local baseAngle = playerAngle - (fovRad / 2)
05106 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         rayStep = fovRad / rayCols
05107 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         stepCos1 = math.cos(rayStep)
05108 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         stepCos2 = math.cos(rayStep * 2)
05109 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         stepCos3 = math.cos(rayStep * 3)
05110 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         stepCos4 = math.cos(rayStep * 4)
05111 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         stepSin1 = math.sin(rayStep)
05112 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         stepSin2 = math.sin(rayStep * 2)
05113 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         stepSin3 = math.sin(rayStep * 3)
05114 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         stepSin4 = math.sin(rayStep * 4)
05115 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         rayCos = math.cos(baseAngle)
05116 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         raySin = math.sin(baseAngle)
05117 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
05118 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     perfMonitorSetRayInfo(basePresetIdx, effectivePresetIdx, useFixedRaycast)
05119 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local wallContactActive = (PLAYER_WALL_CONTACT_FRAMES or 0) > 0
05120 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if wallContactActive then
05121 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         PLAYER_WALL_CONTACT_FRAMES = (PLAYER_WALL_CONTACT_FRAMES or 0) - 1
05122 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
05123 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local stableProjection = (WALL_PROJECTION_MODE == "stable") or wallContactActive
05124 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local nearStabilityDist = WALL_NEAR_STABILITY_DIST or 1.85
05125 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
05126 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     -- Ray-LOD derives from preset steps and keeps mip tiers independent where possible.
05127 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local lodStride1, lodStride2, lodStride3, lodStride4 = 1, 2, 3, 4
05128 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if preset and RAY_PRESETS and #RAY_PRESETS > 0 then
05129 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local baseIdx = effectivePresetIdx
05130 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local baseRays = preset.rays or rayCols
05131 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local function strideFromPresetStep(stepDown)
05132 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local targetIdx = baseIdx - stepDown
05133 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if targetIdx < 1 then targetIdx = 1 end
05134 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local target = RAY_PRESETS[targetIdx]
05135 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local targetRays = target and target.rays or baseRays
05136 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if not targetRays or targetRays < 1 then
05137 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 return 1
05138 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             end
05139 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local s = math.ceil(baseRays / targetRays)
05140 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if s < 1 then s = 1 end
05141 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             return s
05142 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
05143 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local maxStride = 6
05144 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local minFarRays = 3
05145 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if baseRays and baseRays > 0 then
05146 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             maxStride = math.floor(baseRays / minFarRays)
05147 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if maxStride < 1 then maxStride = 1 end
05148 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if maxStride > 6 then maxStride = 6 end
05149 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
05150 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         lodStride1 = strideFromPresetStep(1)
05151 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         lodStride2 = math.max(strideFromPresetStep(2), lodStride1 + 1)
05152 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         lodStride3 = math.max(strideFromPresetStep(3), lodStride2 + 1)
05153 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         lodStride4 = math.max(strideFromPresetStep(4), lodStride3 + 1)
05154 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
05155 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         -- Keep tiers independent and progressively more aggressive.
05156 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if maxStride >= 2 and lodStride1 < 2 then lodStride1 = 2 end
05157 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if maxStride >= 3 and lodStride2 < 3 then lodStride2 = 3 end
05158 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if maxStride >= 4 and lodStride3 < 4 then lodStride3 = 4 end
05159 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if maxStride >= 5 and lodStride4 < 5 then lodStride4 = 5 end
05160 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
05161 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if lodStride1 > maxStride then lodStride1 = maxStride end
05162 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if lodStride2 > maxStride then lodStride2 = maxStride end
05163 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if lodStride3 > maxStride then lodStride3 = maxStride end
05164 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if lodStride4 > maxStride then lodStride4 = maxStride end
05165 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if lodStride2 < lodStride1 then lodStride2 = lodStride1 end
05166 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if lodStride3 < lodStride2 then lodStride3 = lodStride2 end
05167 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if lodStride4 < lodStride3 then lodStride4 = lodStride3 end
05168 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
05169 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
05170 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     -- Mip thresholds are evaluated once per frame so each tier is independent and cheap in the hot ray loop.
05171 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     -- Order is still strictly monotonic for deterministic tier transitions.
05172 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local mip1Thresh = WALL_MIPMAP_DIST1 or 4.0
05173 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local mip2Thresh = WALL_MIPMAP_DIST2 or (mip1Thresh + 2.0)
05174 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local mip3Thresh = WALL_MIPMAP_DIST3 or (mip2Thresh + 2.0)
05175 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local mip4Thresh = WALL_MIPMAP_DIST4 or (mip3Thresh + 2.0)
05176 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if mip2Thresh <= mip1Thresh then mip2Thresh = mip1Thresh + 0.1 end
05177 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if mip3Thresh <= mip2Thresh then mip3Thresh = mip2Thresh + 0.1 end
05178 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if mip4Thresh <= mip3Thresh then mip4Thresh = mip3Thresh + 0.1 end
05179 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
05180 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local x = 0
05181 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     while x < rayCols do
05182 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local rayStride = 1
05183 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local mipLevel = 0
05184 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local castCos, castSin
05185 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local dist, wtype, side, texCoord, rayHit
05186 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local castT0
05187 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if canTime then
05188 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             castT0 = vmupro.system.getTimeUs()
05189 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
05190 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if useFixedRaycast then
05191 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local rayOff = (rayOffsets and rayOffsets[x + 1]) or 0
05192 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local rayDir = (playerDirFix + rayOff) % (EXP_FIXED_DIR_STEPS or 2048)
05193 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             castCos = rayDirCos[rayDir] or playerCos
05194 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             castSin = rayDirSin[rayDir] or playerSin
05195 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             dist, wtype, side, texCoord, rayHit = expCastRayFixed(rayDir, rayTraceDist)
05196 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         else
05197 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             castCos = rayCos
05198 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             castSin = raySin
05199 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             dist, wtype, side, texCoord, rayHit = castRay(castCos, castSin, rayTraceDist)
05200 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
05201 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if canTime and castT0 then
05202 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local castT1 = vmupro.system.getTimeUs()
05203 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             PERF_MONITOR_SAMPLE_RAYCAST_US = (PERF_MONITOR_SAMPLE_RAYCAST_US or 0) + (castT1 - castT0)
05204 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
05205 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local fixedDist = dist * (castCos * playerCos + castSin * playerSin)
05206 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local nearClipDist = getPlayerRenderNearClipDist()
05207 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if fixedDist < nearClipDist then fixedDist = nearClipDist end
05208 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if not rayHit then
05209 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             fixedDist = fogView
05210 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if fixedDist < texView then fixedDist = texView end
05211 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if fixedDist > hybridViewDist then fixedDist = hybridViewDist end

05213 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
05214 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local nearForce = rayHit and (
05215 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             fixedDist < (MIP_NEAR_FORCE_DIST or 1.35)
05216 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             or (wallContactActive and fixedDist < nearStabilityDist)

05219 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if fixedDist >= mip4Thresh then
05220 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 mipLevel = 4
05221 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             elseif fixedDist >= mip3Thresh then
05222 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 mipLevel = 3
05223 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             elseif fixedDist >= mip2Thresh then
05224 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 mipLevel = 2
05225 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             elseif fixedDist >= mip1Thresh then
05226 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 mipLevel = 1
05227 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             end

05231 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 rayStride = lodStride4
05232 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             elseif mipLevel == 3 then
05233 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 rayStride = lodStride3
05234 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             elseif mipLevel == 2 then
05235 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 rayStride = lodStride2
05236 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             elseif mipLevel == 1 then
05237 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 rayStride = lodStride1
05238 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             end

05258 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]

05266 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     elseif mipLevel == 2 then
05267 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                         PERF_MONITOR_MIP_COLS_2 = (PERF_MONITOR_MIP_COLS_2 or 0) + spanW
05268 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     elseif mipLevel == 3 then

05296 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     local baseColor = getWallColor(wtype, side)

05301 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                         local drawT1 = vmupro.system.getTimeUs()

05306 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                             PERF_MONITOR_FOG_COLS = (PERF_MONITOR_FOG_COLS or 0) + spanW

05311 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                             local fogT1 = vmupro.system.getTimeUs()

05313 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                         end

05315 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 else
05316 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     local useTex = texCoord or 0
05317 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     if useTex < 0 then useTex = 0 end
05318 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     if useTex > 0.999 then useTex = 0.999 end

05320 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     if side == 0 and castCos > flipEps then
05321 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                         useTex = 1.0 - useTex
05322 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     elseif side == 1 and castSin < -flipEps then
05323 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                         useTex = 1.0 - useTex
05324 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     end
05325 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     if useTex < 0.001 then useTex = 0.001 end
05326 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     if useTex > 0.998 then useTex = 0.998 end
05327 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     local drewTex = drawWallTextureColumn(wtype, side, useTex, sx, y1, y2, drawColW, fixedDist, mipLevel)
05328 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     if not drewTex then
05329 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                         if trackCounters then
05330 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                             PERF_MONITOR_WALL_COLS_FALLBACK = (PERF_MONITOR_WALL_COLS_FALLBACK or 0) + spanW
05331 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                         end
05332 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                         local baseColor = getWallColor(wtype, side)

05334 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                         if canTime then drawT0 = vmupro.system.getTimeUs() end
05335 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                         vmupro.graphics.drawFillRect(sx, y1, ex, y2, baseColor)
05336 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                         if canTime and drawT0 then
05337 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                             local drawT1 = vmupro.system.getTimeUs()
05338 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                             PERF_MONITOR_SAMPLE_WALL_US = (PERF_MONITOR_SAMPLE_WALL_US or 0) + (drawT1 - drawT0)
05339 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                         end
05340 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                         if fogAlpha > 0 then
05341 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                             if trackCounters then
05342 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                                 PERF_MONITOR_FOG_COLS = (PERF_MONITOR_FOG_COLS or 0) + spanW
05343 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                             end
05344 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                             if canTime then drawT0 = vmupro.system.getTimeUs() end
05345 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                             drawFogOverlayArea(sx, y1, ex, y2, fogAlpha)
05346 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                             if canTime and drawT0 then

05348 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                                 PERF_MONITOR_SAMPLE_FOG_US = (PERF_MONITOR_SAMPLE_FOG_US or 0) + (fogT1 - drawT0)
05349 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                             end
05350 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                         end
05351 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     else
05352 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                         if trackCounters then
05353 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                             PERF_MONITOR_WALL_COLS_TEXTURED = (PERF_MONITOR_WALL_COLS_TEXTURED or 0) + spanW
05354 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                         end
05355 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     end
05356 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 end
05357 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             elseif not rayHit and not DEBUG_DISABLE_FOG then
05358 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 -- Draw a fog curtain when no wall was traced inside draw distance.
05359 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 -- This keeps fog coverage independent from draw-distance cutoff.
05360 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 if trackCounters then
05361 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     PERF_MONITOR_FOG_COLS = (PERF_MONITOR_FOG_COLS or 0) + spanW
05362 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 end
05363 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 local fogT0
05364 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 if canTime then fogT0 = vmupro.system.getTimeUs() end
05365 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 drawFogCurtainColumn(sx, ex, fogView)
05366 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 if canTime and fogT0 then
05367 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     local fogT1 = vmupro.system.getTimeUs()
05368 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     PERF_MONITOR_SAMPLE_FOG_US = (PERF_MONITOR_SAMPLE_FOG_US or 0) + (fogT1 - fogT0)
05369 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 end
05370 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             end
05371 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
05372 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
05373 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if not useFixedRaycast then
05374 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local sc, ss
05375 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if rayStride == 1 then
05376 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 sc, ss = stepCos1, stepSin1
05377 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             elseif rayStride == 2 then
05378 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 sc, ss = stepCos2, stepSin2
05379 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             elseif rayStride == 3 then
05380 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 sc, ss = stepCos3, stepSin3
05381 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             elseif rayStride == 4 then
05382 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 sc, ss = stepCos4, stepSin4
05383 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             else
05384 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 sc = math.cos(rayStep * rayStride)
05385 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 ss = math.sin(rayStep * rayStride)
05386 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             end
05387 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local newCos = rayCos * sc - raySin * ss
05388 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local newSin = raySin * sc + rayCos * ss
05389 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             rayCos, raySin = newCos, newSin
05390 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
05391 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         x = x + rayStride
05392 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
05393 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end
05394 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
05395 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] function castRay(dx, dy, maxDist)
05396 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if dx == 0 and dy == 0 then
05397 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return 16, 1, 0, 0, false
05398 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
05399 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
05400 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local mapX = math.floor(px)
05401 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local mapY = math.floor(py)
05402 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local rayMaxDist = maxDist or 16
05403 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if rayMaxDist < 0.25 then
05404 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         rayMaxDist = 0.25
05405 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
05406 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
05407 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     -- Guard against rare movement penetration: stabilize rendering when inside a wall cell.
05408 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if mapX >= 0 and mapX < 16 and mapY >= 0 and mapY < 16 then
05409 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local startTile = map and map[mapY + 1] and map[mapY + 1][mapX + 1] or 0
05410 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if startTile and startTile > 0 then
05411 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             return getStartSolidRayFallback(px, py, mapX, mapY, startTile)
05412 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
05413 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
05414 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
05415 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local deltaDistX = (dx == 0) and 1e9 or math.abs(1 / dx)
05416 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local deltaDistY = (dy == 0) and 1e9 or math.abs(1 / dy)
05417 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
05418 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local stepX, stepY
05419 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local sideDistX, sideDistY
05420 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
05421 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if dx < 0 then
05422 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         stepX = -1
05423 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         sideDistX = (px - mapX) * deltaDistX
05424 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     else
05425 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         stepX = 1
05426 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         sideDistX = (mapX + 1.0 - px) * deltaDistX
05427 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
05428 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
05429 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if dy < 0 then
05430 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         stepY = -1
05431 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         sideDistY = (py - mapY) * deltaDistY
05432 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     else
05433 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         stepY = 1
05434 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         sideDistY = (mapY + 1.0 - py) * deltaDistY
05435 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
05436 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
05437 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local hit = false
05438 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local side = 0
05439 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     -- PERFORMANCE: Reduced from 64 to 32
05440 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     -- Map is only 16x16, and most rays hit walls well before this limit
05441 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     -- Cuts worst-case raycast iterations by 50% (240 rays  32 = 7,680 vs 15,360)
05442 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local maxSteps = 32
05443 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local wtype = 1
05444 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     for _ = 1, maxSteps do
05445 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local nextDist = sideDistX
05446 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if sideDistY < nextDist then nextDist = sideDistY end
05447 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if nextDist > rayMaxDist then
05448 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             break
05449 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
05450 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if sideDistX < sideDistY then
05451 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             sideDistX = sideDistX + deltaDistX
05452 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             mapX = mapX + stepX
05453 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             side = 0
05454 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         else
05455 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             sideDistY = sideDistY + deltaDistY
05456 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             mapY = mapY + stepY
05457 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             side = 1
05458 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
05459 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if mapX < 0 or mapX >= 16 or mapY < 0 or mapY >= 16 then
05460 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             break
05461 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
05462 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         wtype = map[mapY + 1][mapX + 1]
05463 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if wtype > 0 then
05464 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             hit = true
05465 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             break
05466 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
05467 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
05468 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
05469 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not hit then
05470 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return rayMaxDist, 1, 0, 0, false
05471 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
05472 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
05473 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local perpWallDist
05474 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if side == 0 then
05475 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         perpWallDist = (mapX - px + (1 - stepX) / 2) / (dx == 0 and 1e-6 or dx)
05476 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     else
05477 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         perpWallDist = (mapY - py + (1 - stepY) / 2) / (dy == 0 and 1e-6 or dy)
05478 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
05479 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
05480 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local texCoord
05481 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if side == 0 then
05482 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         texCoord = py + perpWallDist * dy
05483 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     else
05484 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         texCoord = px + perpWallDist * dx
05485 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
05486 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     texCoord = texCoord - math.floor(texCoord)
05487 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if texCoord < 0 then texCoord = texCoord + 1 end
05488 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if texCoord > 0.999 then texCoord = 0.999 end
05489 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
05490 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return perpWallDist, wtype, side, texCoord, true
05491 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end
05492 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
05493 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function isVisible(tx, ty, cache)
05494 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local expRenderer = isExpRenderer()
05495 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local useCache = cache and (not expRenderer)
05496 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if useCache then
05497 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local lastFrame = cache._visFrame or -1000
05498 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if frameCount - lastFrame < 14 then
05499 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             return cache._visValue == true
05500 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
05501 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
05502 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local dx, dy = tx - px, ty - py
05503 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local dist = math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy)
05504 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local maxDist = SPRITE_VIS_DIST or 6
05505 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if expRenderer then
05506 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local viewDist = EXP_VIEW_DIST or maxDist
05507 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if viewDist < maxDist then maxDist = viewDist end
05508 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
05509 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if dist > maxDist then
05510 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if useCache then
05511 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             cache._visFrame = frameCount
05512 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             cache._visValue = false
05513 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
05514 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return false
05515 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
05516 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if expRenderer then
05517 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local dir = pdir % 64
05518 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local cosDir = cosTable[dir]
05519 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local sinDir = sinTable[dir]
05520 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local relX = dx * sinDir - dy * cosDir
05521 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local relY = dx * cosDir + dy * sinDir
05522 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if relY <= 0.05 then
05523 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if useCache then
05524 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 cache._visFrame = frameCount
05525 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 cache._visValue = false
05526 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             end
05527 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             return false
05528 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
05529 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local fovRad = renderCfg.fovSteps * (renderCfg.twoPi / 64)
05530 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local maxSx = math.tan(fovRad / 2)
05531 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local sx = relX / relY
05532 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if sx < -maxSx or sx > maxSx then
05533 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if useCache then
05534 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 cache._visFrame = frameCount
05535 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 cache._visValue = false
05536 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             end
05537 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             return false
05538 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
05539 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
05540 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if dist < 0.1 then
05541 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if useCache then
05542 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             cache._visFrame = frameCount
05543 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             cache._visValue = true
05544 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
05545 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return true
05546 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
05547 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     dx, dy = dx / dist, dy / dist
05548 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local rx, ry, traveled = px, py, 0
05549 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local step = expRenderer and 0.1 or 0.25
05550 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     while traveled < dist - step do
05551 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         rx, ry = rx + dx * step, ry + dy * step
05552 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         traveled = traveled + step
05553 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local mx, my = math.floor(rx), math.floor(ry)
05554 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if mx >= 0 and mx < 16 and my >= 0 and my < 16 then
05555 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if map[my + 1][mx + 1] > 0 then
05556 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 if useCache then
05557 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     cache._visFrame = frameCount
05558 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     cache._visValue = false
05559 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 end
05560 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 return false
05561 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             end
05562 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             -- Thicken the ray to avoid corner peeking
05563 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local r = 0.1
05564 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local mx1, mx2 = math.floor(rx - r), math.floor(rx + r)
05565 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local my1, my2 = math.floor(ry - r), math.floor(ry + r)
05566 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if mx1 < 0 or mx2 >= 16 or my1 < 0 or my2 >= 16 then
05567 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 if useCache then
05568 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     cache._visFrame = frameCount
05569 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     cache._visValue = false
05570 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 end
05571 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 return false
05572 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             end
05573 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if map[my1 + 1][mx1 + 1] > 0 or map[my1 + 1][mx2 + 1] > 0
05574 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 or map[my2 + 1][mx1 + 1] > 0 or map[my2 + 1][mx2 + 1] > 0 then
05575 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 if useCache then
05576 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     cache._visFrame = frameCount
05577 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     cache._visValue = false
05578 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 end
05579 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 return false
05580 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             end
05581 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
05582 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
05583 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if useCache then
05584 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         cache._visFrame = frameCount
05585 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         cache._visValue = true
05586 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
05587 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return true
05588 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end

05590 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function drawSprite(screenX, dist, stype, viewAngle, animFrame, spriteData)
05591 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if dist < 0.3 then return end
05592 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local size = math.floor(100 / dist)
05593 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if size < 6 then return end
05594 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if size > 140 then size = 140 end
05595 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]

05600 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if groundY > VIEWPORT_H then groundY = VIEWPORT_H end

05602 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]

05607 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]

05610 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local tw = math.floor(size / 5)

05712 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         -- Warrior Guard using real sprites

05989 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]

05991 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
05992 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
05993 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     elseif stype == 7 then
05994 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         -- Health vial pickup (uses potion sprite)
05995 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if spriteData and spriteData.collected then
05996 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             return  -- Don't draw collected vials
05997 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
05998 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
05999 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if potionSprite and potionSprite.height then
06000 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             -- Scale potion to fit on ground
06001 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local desiredHeight = size * 0.6  -- Smaller than characters
06002 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local scale = desiredHeight / potionSprite.height
06003 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
06004 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local scaledWidth = potionSprite.width * scale
06005 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local scaledHeight = potionSprite.height * scale
06006 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local drawX = screenX - math.floor(scaledWidth / 2)
06007 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
06008 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             -- Position on ground
06009 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local groundY = HORIZON + size
06010 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if groundY > 240 then groundY = 240 end
06011 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local drawY = groundY - math.floor(scaledHeight)
06012 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
06013 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             vmupro.sprite.drawScaled(potionSprite, drawX, drawY, scale, scale, vmupro.sprite.kImageUnflipped)
06014 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
06015 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
06016 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end
06017 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
06018 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function drawRoofBackdrop()
06019 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local roofBottom = HORIZON - 1
06020 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if roofBottom < 0 then
06021 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return
06022 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
06023 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
06024 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     -- Single-image ceiling over the full map roof.
06025 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     -- Map anchors are computed in camera space so this behaves like a world roof,
06026 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     -- not a static screen overlay.
06027 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local roofTex = nil
06028 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not DEBUG_DISABLE_WALL_TEXTURE and not DEBUG_DISABLE_ROOF_TEXTURE then
06029 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         roofTex = wallRoof or wallBrick
06030 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
06031 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if roofTex and validateSprite(roofTex, "drawRoofBackdrop") then
06032 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local texW = roofTex.width or 128
06033 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local texH = roofTex.height or 128
06034 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if texW < 1 then texW = 1 end
06035 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if texH < 1 then texH = 1 end
06036 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
06037 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local mapW = 16
06038 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local mapH = 16
06039 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if map and #map > 0 then
06040 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             mapH = #map
06041 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if map[1] and #map[1] > 0 then
06042 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 mapW = #map[1]
06043 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             end
06044 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
06045 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if mapW < 1 then mapW = 16 end
06046 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if mapH < 1 then mapH = 16 end
06047 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
06048 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         -- Stretch one image across full map space (large stretch by design).
06049 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local stretchPxPerTileX = 32
06050 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local stretchPxPerTileY = 24
06051 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local targetW = 240 + (mapW * stretchPxPerTileX)
06052 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local targetH = (roofBottom + 1) + (mapH * stretchPxPerTileY)
06053 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local panRangeX = targetW - 240
06054 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local panRangeY = targetH - (roofBottom + 1)
06055 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if panRangeX < 0 then panRangeX = 0 end
06056 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if panRangeY < 0 then panRangeY = 0 end
06057 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
06058 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local ang = ((pdir or 0) % 64) * (renderCfg.twoPi / 64)
06059 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local ca = math.cos(ang)
06060 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local sa = math.sin(ang)
06061 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
06062 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         -- Camera-space axes:
06063 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         -- forward = dot(world, viewDir), lateral = dot(world, rightDir)
06064 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local function projectForward(x, y)
06065 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             return (x * ca) + (y * sa)
06066 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
06067 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local function projectLateral(x, y)
06068 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             return (-x * sa) + (y * ca)
06069 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
06070 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
06071 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local c1x, c1y = 0, 0
06072 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local c2x, c2y = mapW, 0
06073 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local c3x, c3y = 0, mapH
06074 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local c4x, c4y = mapW, mapH
06075 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local f1, f2 = projectForward(c1x, c1y), projectForward(c2x, c2y)
06076 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local f3, f4 = projectForward(c3x, c3y), projectForward(c4x, c4y)
06077 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local l1, l2 = projectLateral(c1x, c1y), projectLateral(c2x, c2y)
06078 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local l3, l4 = projectLateral(c3x, c3y), projectLateral(c4x, c4y)
06079 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
06080 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local minFwd = math.min(f1, f2, f3, f4)
06081 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local maxFwd = math.max(f1, f2, f3, f4)
06082 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local minLat = math.min(l1, l2, l3, l4)
06083 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local maxLat = math.max(l1, l2, l3, l4)
06084 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
06085 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local curFwd = projectForward((px or 0), (py or 0))
06086 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local curLat = projectLateral((px or 0), (py or 0))
06087 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local fwdSpan = maxFwd - minFwd
06088 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local latSpan = maxLat - minLat
06089 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if fwdSpan < 0.001 then fwdSpan = 0.001 end
06090 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if latSpan < 0.001 then latSpan = 0.001 end
06091 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
06092 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local nx = safeDivide((curLat - minLat), latSpan, "drawRoofBackdrop_nx")
06093 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local ny = safeDivide((curFwd - minFwd), fwdSpan, "drawRoofBackdrop_ny")
06094 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if nx < 0 then nx = 0 elseif nx > 1 then nx = 1 end
06095 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if ny < 0 then ny = 0 elseif ny > 1 then ny = 1 end
06096 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
06097 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local drawX = -math.floor((nx * panRangeX) + 0.5)
06098 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local drawY = -math.floor((ny * panRangeY) + 0.5)
06099 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
06100 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local scaleX = safeDivide(targetW, texW, "drawRoofBackdrop_scaleX")
06101 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local scaleY = safeDivide(targetH, texH, "drawRoofBackdrop_scaleY")
06102 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if safeScale(roofTex, scaleX, scaleY, "drawRoofBackdrop") then
06103 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             vmupro.sprite.drawScaled(roofTex, drawX, drawY, scaleX, scaleY, vmupro.sprite.kImageUnflipped)
06104 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         else
06105 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             vmupro.graphics.drawFillRect(0, 0, 239, roofBottom, COLOR_DARK_GRAY)
06106 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
06107 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     else
06108 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         vmupro.graphics.drawFillRect(0, 0, 239, roofBottom, COLOR_DARK_GRAY)
06109 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
06110 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
06111 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     -- Keep a strong horizon seam for depth readability against fog.
06112 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     vmupro.graphics.drawLine(0, roofBottom, 239, roofBottom, COLOR_BLACK)
06113 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end
06114 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
06115 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function renderGameFrame()
06116 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     recoverPlayerFromWallPenetration()
06117 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     -- Keep world rendering live while menu is open for real-time tuning.
06118 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local freezeMenuView = false
06119 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not freezeMenuView then
06120 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         -- Game rendering
06121 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         vmupro.graphics.clear(COLOR_CEILING)
06122 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         drawRoofBackdrop()
06123 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         -- Draw floor after roof so any sprite-scale bleed never reaches the floor.
06124 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         vmupro.graphics.drawFillRect(0, HORIZON, 240, VIEWPORT_H, COLOR_FLOOR)
06125 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         vmupro.graphics.drawFillRect(0, VIEWPORT_H, 240, 240, COLOR_BLACK)
06126 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
06127 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
06128 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         -- Single renderer runtime path: EXP-H only.
06129 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         lockRendererMode()
06130 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         renderWallsExperimentalHybrid()
06131 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
06132 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not DEBUG_SKIP_SPRITES and not showMenu then
06133 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if frameCount - spriteOrderCacheFrame >= 8 or #spriteOrderCache == 0 then
06134 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local spriteOrder = {}
06135 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local count = 0
06136 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             for i = 1, #sprites do
06137 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 local s = sprites[i]
06138 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 if not s then
06139 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     goto continue_sprite_build
06140 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 end
06141 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 local skip = (DEBUG_DISABLE_ENEMIES and isEnemyType(s.t))
06142 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     or (DEBUG_DISABLE_PROPS and isPropType(s.t))
06143 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 if not skip then
06144 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     local sdx, sdy = s.x - px, s.y - py
06145 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     local distSq = sdx * sdx + sdy * sdy
06146 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     local maxSq = SPRITE_MAX_DIST_SQ
06147 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     if isEnemyType(s.t) then
06148 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                         maxSq = ENEMY_RENDER_DIST_SQ
06149 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     elseif s.t == 7 then
06150 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                         maxSq = ITEM_RENDER_DIST_SQ
06151 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     elseif isPropType(s.t) then
06152 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                         maxSq = PROP_RENDER_DIST_SQ
06153 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     end
06154 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     if distSq <= maxSq then
06155 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                         count = count + 1
06156 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                         spriteOrder[count] = {idx = i, dist = distSq}
06157 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     end
06158 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 end
06159 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 ::continue_sprite_build::
06160 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             end
06161 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if count > 1 then
06162 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 table.sort(spriteOrder, function(a, b) return a.dist > b.dist end)
06163 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             end
06164 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             spriteOrderCache = spriteOrder
06165 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             spriteOrderCacheFrame = frameCount
06166 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
06167 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
06168 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         for i = 1, #spriteOrderCache do
06169 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local s = sprites[spriteOrderCache[i].idx]
06170 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if not s then
06171 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 goto continue_sprite
06172 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             end
06173 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if DEBUG_DISABLE_ENEMIES and isEnemyType(s.t) then
06174 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 goto continue_sprite
06175 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             end
06176 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if DEBUG_DISABLE_PROPS and isPropType(s.t) then
06177 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 goto continue_sprite
06178 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             end
06179 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             -- Skip dead soldiers
06180 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if s.t == 5 and s.alive == false and not s.dying then
06181 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 goto continue_sprite
06182 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             end
06183 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local sdx, sdy = s.x - px, s.y - py
06184 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local distSq = sdx * sdx + sdy * sdy
06185 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local maxSq = SPRITE_MAX_DIST_SQ
06186 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if isEnemyType(s.t) then
06187 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 maxSq = ENEMY_RENDER_DIST_SQ
06188 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             elseif s.t == 7 then
06189 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 maxSq = ITEM_RENDER_DIST_SQ
06190 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             elseif isPropType(s.t) then
06191 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 maxSq = PROP_RENDER_DIST_SQ
06192 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             end
06193 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if distSq <= maxSq then
06194 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 local sdist = math.sqrt(distSq)
06195 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 local visible = true
06196 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 if sdist > SPRITE_VIS_DIST then
06197 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     visible = false
06198 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 else
06199 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     visible = isVisible(s.x, s.y, s)
06200 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 end
06201 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 if sdist > 0.3 and visible then
06202 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 local sAngle = 0
06203 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 if sdx ~= 0 then
06204 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     sAngle = math.atan(sdy / sdx)
06205 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     if sdx < 0 then sAngle = sAngle + 3.14159 end
06206 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 else
06207 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     sAngle = sdy > 0 and 1.5708 or -1.5708
06208 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 end
06209 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 local sDir = math.floor(sAngle * 64 / 6.28318) % 64
06210 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 local viewDiff = (sDir - pdir) % 64
06211 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 if viewDiff > 32 then viewDiff = viewDiff - 64 end
06212 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 if viewDiff >= -6 and viewDiff <= 6 then
06213 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     if isExpRenderer() then
06214 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                         local dir = pdir % 64
06215 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                         local cosDir = cosTable[dir]
06216 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                         local sinDir = sinTable[dir]
06217 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                         local relX = (sdx * sinDir - sdy * cosDir)
06218 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                         local relY = (sdx * cosDir + sdy * sinDir)
06219 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                         if relY > 0.05 then
06220 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                             local sx = relX / relY
06221 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                             local screenX = math.floor(120 + sx * 120)
06222 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                             local occluded = false
06223 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                             for ox = -2, 2 do
06224 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                                 local cx = screenX + ox
06225 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                                 if cx >= 0 and cx <= 239 then
06226 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                                     local wallDist = expDepthBuf[cx]
06227 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                                     if wallDist and relY > wallDist then
06228 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                                         occluded = true
06229 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                                         break
06230 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                                     end
06231 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                                 end
06232 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                             end
06233 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                             if occluded then
06234 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                                 goto continue_sprite
06235 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                             end
06236 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                         end
06237 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     end
06238 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     -- Calculate view angle for guards (angle from guard's POV)
06239 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     local guardViewAngle = nil
06240 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     if (s.t == 5 or s.t == 6) and s.dir then
06241 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                         -- Angle player is approaching from relative to guard's facing
06242 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                         local approachDir = (sDir + 32) % 64  -- Opposite of sDir
06243 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                         guardViewAngle = (approachDir - s.dir) % 64
06244 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                         if guardViewAngle > 32 then guardViewAngle = guardViewAngle - 64 end
06245 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     end
06246 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     drawSprite(120 + viewDiff * 20, sdist, s.t, guardViewAngle, s.anim, s)
06247 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 end
06248 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 end
06249 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             end
06250 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             ::continue_sprite::
06251 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             end
06252 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end

06465 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
06466 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function consumeAudioSteps(elapsedUs, audioAccumulatorUs)
06467 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if not audioSystemActive or not soundEnabled then
06468 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return 0.0, 0
06469 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
06470 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
06471 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local dt = elapsedUs or AUDIO_UPDATE_STEP_US
06472 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if dt < 0 then
06473 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         dt = AUDIO_UPDATE_STEP_US
06474 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
06475 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if dt > 250000 then
06476 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         dt = 250000
06477 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
06478 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
06479 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local acc = (audioAccumulatorUs or 0) + dt
06480 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local maxBacklog = AUDIO_UPDATE_STEP_US * (AUDIO_UPDATE_MAX_BACKLOG_STEPS or 3)
06481 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if acc > maxBacklog then
06482 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         acc = maxBacklog
06483 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
06484 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
06485 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local steps = 0
06486 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     while acc >= AUDIO_UPDATE_STEP_US and steps < (AUDIO_UPDATE_MAX_STEPS or 3) do
06487 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         vmupro.sound.update()
06488 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         acc = acc - AUDIO_UPDATE_STEP_US
06489 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         steps = steps + 1
06490 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
06491 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
06492 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return acc, steps
06493 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end
06494 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
06495 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function runSimulationStep()
06496 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     simTickCount = simTickCount + 1
06497 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if saveMenuMessageTimer and saveMenuMessageTimer > 0 then
06498 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         saveMenuMessageTimer = saveMenuMessageTimer - 1
06499 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
06500 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
06501 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if gameState == STATE_PLAYING and not showMenu then
06502 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if levelBannerTimer > 0 then
06503 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             levelBannerTimer = levelBannerTimer - 1
06504 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
06505 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if isAttacking > 0 then
06506 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             isAttacking = isAttacking - 1
06507 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
06508 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         updateSoldiers()
06509 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         updateDeathAnimations()
06510 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if not DEBUG_DISABLE_EFFECTS then
06511 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             updateBloodEffects()
06512 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
06513 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         checkHealthPickups()
06514 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     elseif gameState == STATE_LOADING then
06515 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         loadingTimer = loadingTimer - 1
06516 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if loadingTimer <= 0 then
06517 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if pendingLevelStart then

06520 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             else
06521 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 gameState = STATE_TITLE
06522 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             end
06523 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
06524 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     elseif gameState == STATE_WIN then
06525 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if winBannerTimer > 0 then
06526 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             winBannerTimer = winBannerTimer - 1
06527 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
06528 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if winCooldown > 0 then
06529 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             winCooldown = winCooldown - 1
06530 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
06531 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
06532 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end
06533 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
06534 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] local function consumeSimulationSteps(elapsedUs, simAccumulatorUs)
06535 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if gameState ~= STATE_PLAYING and gameState ~= STATE_LOADING and gameState ~= STATE_WIN then
06536 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         return 0.0, 0
06537 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
06538 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
06539 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local dt = elapsedUs or SIM_STEP_US
06540 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if dt < 0 then
06541 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         dt = SIM_STEP_US
06542 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
06543 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if dt > 250000 then
06544 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         dt = 250000
06545 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
06546 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
06547 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local acc = (simAccumulatorUs or 0) + dt
06548 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local maxBacklog = SIM_STEP_US * (SIM_MAX_BACKLOG_STEPS or 4)
06549 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     if acc > maxBacklog then
06550 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         acc = maxBacklog
06551 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
06552 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
06553 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     local steps = 0
06554 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     while acc >= SIM_STEP_US and steps < (SIM_MAX_STEPS_PER_FRAME or 4) do
06555 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         runSimulationStep()
06556 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         acc = acc - SIM_STEP_US
06557 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         steps = steps + 1
06558 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if gameState == STATE_TITLE then
06559 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             acc = 0.0
06560 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             break
06561 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
06562 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
06563 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
06564 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return acc, steps
06565 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end
