07298 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 quitApp("render error: " .. tostring(errRender))
07299 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             end
07300 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end  -- End of game rendering (else branch of title screen check)
07301 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if renderSectionStartUs and perfSectionClock then
07302 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local renderSectionEndUs = perfSectionClock()
07303 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if renderSectionEndUs and renderSectionEndUs >= renderSectionStartUs then
07304 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 PERF_MONITOR_SAMPLE_RENDER_US = PERF_MONITOR_SAMPLE_RENDER_US + (renderSectionEndUs - renderSectionStartUs)
07305 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             end
07306 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
07307 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
07308 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         ::render_only::
07309 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         local presentSectionStartUs = perfSectionClock and perfSectionClock()
07310 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         presentFrame()
07311 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if presentSectionStartUs and perfSectionClock then
07312 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local presentSectionEndUs = perfSectionClock()
07313 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if presentSectionEndUs and presentSectionEndUs >= presentSectionStartUs then
07314 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 PERF_MONITOR_SAMPLE_PRESENT_US = PERF_MONITOR_SAMPLE_PRESENT_US + (presentSectionEndUs - presentSectionStartUs)
07315 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             end
07316 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
07317 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if gameState == STATE_TITLE then
07318 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             targetFrameUs = 16667
07319 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         else
07320 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if FPS_TARGET_MODE == "uncapped" then
07321 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 targetFrameUs = 0
07322 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             elseif FPS_TARGET_MODE == "60" then
07323 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 targetFrameUs = 16667
07324 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             elseif FPS_TARGET_MODE == "45" then
07325 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 targetFrameUs = 22222
07326 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             elseif FPS_TARGET_MODE == "30" then
07327 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 targetFrameUs = 33333
07328 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             elseif FPS_TARGET_MODE == "24" then
07329 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 targetFrameUs = 41667
07330 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             else
07331 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 targetFrameUs = 33333
07332 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             end
07333 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
07334 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         if vmupro.system and vmupro.system.getTimeUs then
07335 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             local frameEndUs = vmupro.system.getTimeUs()
07336 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             if frameStartUs > 0 and frameEndUs > frameStartUs then
07337 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 local cpuElapsedUs = frameEndUs - frameStartUs
07338 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 local remainingUs = targetFrameUs - cpuElapsedUs
07339 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 if remainingUs > 0 and vmupro.system.delayMs then
07340 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     local sleepSectionStartUs = perfSectionClock and perfSectionClock()
07341 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     vmupro.system.delayMs(math.floor(remainingUs / 1000))
07342 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     if sleepSectionStartUs and perfSectionClock then
07343 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                         local sleepSectionEndUs = perfSectionClock()
07344 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                         if sleepSectionEndUs and sleepSectionEndUs >= sleepSectionStartUs then
07345 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                             PERF_MONITOR_SAMPLE_SLEEP_US = PERF_MONITOR_SAMPLE_SLEEP_US + (sleepSectionEndUs - sleepSectionStartUs)
07346 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                         end
07347 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                     end
07348 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 end
07349 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 local perfNowUsAfterSleep = vmupro.system.getTimeUs()
07350 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]                 perfMonitorEndFrame(cpuElapsedUs, perfNowUsAfterSleep)
07351 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]             end
07352 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]         end
07353 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     end
07354 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
07355 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     -- Cleanup assets
07356 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     applyDoubleBufferMode(false)
07357 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     unloadLevelAudio()
07358 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     unloadLevelSprites()
07359 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     unloadMenuSprites()
07360 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] 
07361 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING]     return 0
07362 [GPT-5-CODEX-MAX-REASONING] end
